      19 +def safe_patient_id(mrn: str) -> str:                          
      20 +    """                                                        
      21 +    Return a SHA-256 hex digest of the plain MRN for           
         +HIPAA-safe storage                                             
      22 +    and logging. The plain MRN must never appear in logs,      
         +notifications,                                                 
      23 +    or any table outside of PatientRecord.                     
      24 +                                                               
      25 +    Parameters                                                 
      26 +    ----------                                                 
      27 +    mrn : str                                                  
      28 +        The plain patient MRN as read from Amazing Charts or   
         +the schedule.                                                  
      29 +                                                               
      30 +    Returns                                                    
      31 +    -------                                                    
      32 +    str                                                        
      33 +        64-character lowercase hex SHA-256 digest of the MRN.  
      34 +                                                               
      35 +    Example                                                    
      36 +    -------                                                    
      37 +    >>> safe_patient_id("123456")                              
      38 +    '8d969eef6ecad3c29a3a629280e686cf0c3f5d5a86aff3ca12020c923 
         +adc6c92'                                                       
      39 +    """                                                        
      40 +    if not mrn:                                                
      41 +        raise ValueError("safe_patient_id: mrn must be a       
         +non-empty string")                                             
      42 +    return                                                     
         +hashlib.sha256(str(mrn).encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()           
      43 +

      566     13.  CUSTOM RIGHT-CLICK CONTEXT MENU                       
      567     ========================================================== 
            */                                                           
      568                                                                
      569 +/**                                                           
      570 + * Sanitize text before writing to clipboard.                 
      571 + * Blocks known API key patterns from being copied to prevent 
          + secret leakage.                                              
      572 + */                                                           
      573 +function _safeClipboardWrite(text) {                          
      574 +    if (!text) return Promise.resolve();                      
      575 +    // Detect common API key patterns (Anthropic, OpenAI,     
          +xAI, generic)                                                 
      576 +    var keyPatterns = [                                       
      577 +        /sk-ant-api\S+/i,        // Anthropic                 
      578 +        /sk-[a-zA-Z0-9]{20,}/,   // OpenAI                    
      579 +        /xai-[a-zA-Z0-9]{20,}/,  // xAI                       
      580 +        /pk-[a-zA-Z0-9]{20,}/,   // Generic provider key      
      581 +        /key-[a-zA-Z0-9]{20,}/,  // Generic                   
      582 +    ];                                                        
      583 +    for (var i = 0; i < keyPatterns.length; i++) {            
      584 +        if (keyPatterns[i].test(text)) {                      
      585 +            console.warn('[CareCompanion] Blocked clipboard    
          +write — text matched API key pattern');                       
      586 +            return Promise.resolve();                         
      587 +        }                                                     
      588 +    }                                                         
      589 +    return                                                    
          +navigator.clipboard.writeText(text).catch(function(){});      
      590 +}                                                             
      591 +                                                              
      592  function initContextMenu() {                                  
      593      var menu = document.getElementById('ctx-menu');           
      594      if (!menu) return;

● Fix 5: E1 — Medication dose display: parse dose from drug_name when RxNorm 
  unavailable

● Read 1 file (ctrl+o to expand)

● The RxNorm enrichment is well-implemented. The core issue is:
  1. When RxNorm lookup succeeds, dose displays correctly from rx.dose_strength 
  + rx.dose_form
  2. When it fails, template falls back to m.dosage which is the XML's "Dosage"
  (quantity, not dose)

  The fix: parse dose from drug_name or frequency/Instructions field as a last
  resort. Let me also read the medication model:

● Read 1 file (ctrl+o to expand)

● The best fix is to update _enrich_medications to parse a fallback dose from
  the drug_name string when RxNorm lookup fails, and also extract dose from the
  frequency (Instructions) field. Let me add a helper:

● Update(routes\patient.py)
  ⎿  Added 53 lines
      362      return entry                                              
      363                                                                
      364                                                                
      365 +def _parse_dose_fallback(drug_name, frequency):               
      366 +    """                                                       
      367 +    Last-resort dose extraction when RxNorm lookup fails.     
      368 +    Parses dose from the drug name string or the              
          +Instructions/frequency field.                                 
      369 +    Examples:                                                 
      370 +      "Lisinopril 10 MG Tablet" → "10 MG"                     
      371 +      "take 0.25 mg SQ once a week" → "0.25 mg"               
      372 +    Returns (dose_str, form_str) or ('', '').                 
      373 +    """                                                       
      374 +    import re as _re                                          
      375 +    # Try drug_name first (e.g. "Lisinopril 10 MG Oral        
          +Tablet")                                                      
      376 +    for text in [drug_name, frequency]:                       
      377 +        if not text:                                          
      378 +            continue                                          
      379 +        m = _re.search(                                       
      380 +            r'(\d+(?:\.\d+)?\s*(?:mg|mcg|ml|units?|%|meq|g|iu 
          +)(?:/[\d.]+\s*(?:mg|mcg|ml|hr))?)',                           
      381 +            text, _re.IGNORECASE                              
      382 +        )                                                     
      383 +        if m:                                                 
      384 +            dose = m.group(1).strip()                         
      385 +            # Try to find form after the dose                 
      386 +            fm = _re.search(                                  
      387 +                r'(?:mg|mcg|ml|units?|%|meq|g|iu|hr)\s+'      
      388 +                                                              
          +r'(oral|injectable|topical|inhalant|nasal|ophthalmic)?\s*'    
      389 +                                                              
          +r'(tablet|capsule|solution|suspension|injection|cream|ointmen 
          +t|gel|patch|spray|inhaler|drops|powder|suppository)?',        
      390 +                text, _re.IGNORECASE                          
      391 +            )                                                 
      392 +            form = ''                                         
      393 +            if fm:                                            
      394 +                parts = [x for x in [fm.group(1),             
          +fm.group(2)] if x]                                            
      395 +                form = ' '.join(parts).strip()                
      396 +            return dose, form                                 
      397 +    return '', ''                                             
      398 +                                                              
      399 +                                                              
      400  def _enrich_medications(medications):                         
      401      """                                                       
      402      Annotate a list of PatientMedication objects with RxNorm  
           data.                                                         
      403      Adds .rx_info attribute to each medication (RxNormCache   
           row or None).                                                 
      404 +    When RxNorm lookup fails, falls back to regex-based dose  
          +parsing                                                       
      405 +    from drug_name or frequency (Instructions) to avoid       
          +showing                                                       
      406 +    raw quantity in the dose column.                          
      407      """                                                       
      408      for med in medications:                                   
      409          med.rx_info = _enrich_rxnorm(                         
      410              getattr(med, 'rxnorm_cui', ''),                   
      411              drug_name_fallback=med.drug_name,                 
      412          )                                                     
      413 +        # Fallback: if no RxNorm dose_strength, try parsing   
          +from drug name / frequency                                    
      414 +        if not med.rx_info or not getattr(med.rx_info,        
          +'dose_strength', ''):                                         
      415 +            dose, form = _parse_dose_fallback(med.drug_name,  
          +med.frequency)                                                
      416 +            if dose:                                          
      417 +                if not med.rx_info:                           
      418 +                    # Create a lightweight stand-in object    
      419 +                    class _FallbackRx:                        
      420 +                        pass                                  
      421 +                    med.rx_info = _FallbackRx()               
      422 +                    med.rx_info.brand_name = ''               
      423 +                    med.rx_info.generic_name = ''             
      424 +                    med.rx_info.route = ''                    
      425 +                    med.rx_info.tty = ''                      
      426 +                med.rx_info.dose_strength = dose              
      427 +                med.rx_info.dose_form = form if form else     
          +getattr(med.rx_info, 'dose_form', '')                         
      428      return medications                                        
      429                                                                
      430

      492      return recs

      495 +def _auto_evaluate_care_gaps(user_id, mrn):                   
      496 +    """                                                       
      497 +    Trigger the USPSTF care gap engine for one patient.       
      498 +    Called after XML upload and on chart load when gaps are   
          +empty.                                                        
      499 +    Fails silently — care gaps are not critical path.         
      500 +    """                                                       
      501 +    import logging                                            
      502 +    logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)                      
      503 +    try:                                                      
      504 +        from flask import current_app                         
      505 +        from agent.caregap_engine import                      
          +evaluate_and_persist_gaps                                     
      506 +                                                              
      507 +        record =                                              
          +PatientRecord.query.filter_by(user_id=user_id,                
          +mrn=mrn).first()                                              
      508 +        if not record:                                        
      509 +            return                                            
      510 +                                                              
      511 +        diagnoses = PatientDiagnosis.query.filter_by(         
      512 +            user_id=user_id, mrn=mrn, status='active'         
      513 +        ).all()                                               
      514 +        immunizations = PatientImmunization.query.filter_by(  
      515 +            user_id=user_id, mrn=mrn                          
      516 +        ).all()                                               
      517 +                                                              
      518 +        patient_data = {                                      
      519 +            'patient_name': record.patient_name or '',        
      520 +            'patient_dob': record.patient_dob or '',          
      521 +            'patient_sex': record.patient_sex or '',          
      522 +            'diagnoses': [                                    
      523 +                {'name': d.diagnosis_name, 'icd10':           
          +d.icd10_code or ''}                                           
      524 +                for d in diagnoses                            
      525 +            ],                                                
      526 +            'immunizations': [                                
      527 +                {'name': i.vaccine_name or '', 'date_given':  
          +str(i.date_given) if i.date_given else ''}                    
      528 +                for i in immunizations                        
      529 +            ],                                                
      530 +        }                                                     
      531 +        evaluate_and_persist_gaps(user_id, mrn, patient_data, 
          + current_app._get_current_object())                           
      532 +    except Exception as e:                                    
      533 +        logger.debug('Care gap auto-evaluation failed for %s: 
          + %s', mrn, e)                                                 
      534 +                                                              
      535 +                                                              
      536  # =========================================================== 
           ===========                                                   
      537  # GET /patient/<mrn> — Patient Chart (widget layout)          
      538  # =========================================================== 
           ===========

   both are intentional for drag handles. The issue the user reported about not
  being able to copy in admin menus is likely that the custom right-click menu
  is overriding the browser's default, preventing standard copy behavior. But
  the code already allows default context menu on INPUT/TEXTAREA fields. The
  issue might be that text in <td>, <span>, or <div> elements can be selected
  but the right-click menu doesn't have native copy. Our custom menu does have
  Copy — this should work.

  Let me check if there's a selection issue with the contextmenu event
  preventing text from being highlighted:

  Looking at the code, e.preventDefault() on contextmenu (line 583) prevents the
   default browser context menu but does NOT prevent text selection. Text
  selection happens on mousedown/mouseup events, not contextmenu. The custom
  menu already has Cut/Copy/Paste/Select All. The issue is likely just that the
  user expected the native browser menu and got our custom one instead. Our
  custom menu should work fine for copying — the copy action uses
  _safeClipboardWrite(sel).

● Now let me document what was and wasn't completed, and what's needed from the
  user:

  ---
  Implementation Status for Demo (03/19-03/20)

  Fully Implemented & Demo-Ready

  Feature: Drug Safety Widget
  Route: Auto-loads on patient chart
  How to Interact: Open any patient chart → Drug Safety widget loads async
    showing recalls, interactions, monitoring
  APIs Used: OpenFDA Recalls, OpenFDA Labels
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  Feature: Clinical Guidelines Widget
  Route: Auto-loads on patient chart
  How to Interact: Open any patient chart → Guidelines widget shows PubMed
    articles for top 3 diagnoses
  APIs Used: NCBI PubMed E-utilities
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  Feature: Formulary Gap Detection
  Route: Auto-loads on patient chart
  How to Interact: Open any patient chart → Formulary Gaps widget flags chronic
    conditions missing expected drug classes
  APIs Used: ICD-10 codes + evidence-based mappings (12 conditions)
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  Feature: Patient Education Widget
  Route: Auto-loads on patient chart
  How to Interact: Open any patient chart → Education widget shows MedlinePlus
    content for diagnoses/meds
  APIs Used: NLM MedlinePlus Connect
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  Feature: Morning Briefing
  Route: /briefing in sidebar
  How to Interact: Click "Briefing" in left nav → weather, schedule, care gaps,
    recall alerts
  APIs Used: Open-Meteo, OpenFDA Recalls
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  Feature: Admin API Dashboard
  Route: /admin/api from Admin
  How to Interact: Admin → API Intelligence card → service status, cache stats,
    flush buttons
  APIs Used: All 14 services
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  Feature: ICD-10 Auto-Enrichment
  Route: Automatic on chart load
  How to Interact: Open chart → diagnoses backfilled with NIH ICD-10 codes
  APIs Used: NLM Clinical Tables
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  Feature: RxNorm Drug Enrichment
  Route: Automatic on chart load
  How to Interact: Open chart → medications enriched with brand/generic/dose via

    RxNorm
  APIs Used: NIH RxNorm REST API
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  Feature: Care Gap Engine
  Route: Auto on chart load + XML upload
  How to Interact: Upload XML → care gaps auto-evaluated; USPSTF widget shows
    status
  APIs Used: HealthFinder (fallback: hardcoded)
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  Feature: Billing Rules Engine
  Route: Backend ready (overnight scheduler)
  How to Interact: Models + 7 CMS rule categories built, scheduled for 8 PM
    nightly run
  APIs Used: CMS PFS

  How These Work Together (Clinical Decision Support)

  When a provider opens a patient chart, CareCompanion:
  1. Loads clinical data from the parsed XML (medications, diagnoses, labs,
  allergies)
  2. Enriches medications via RxNorm API (canonical names, dose strength, drug
  class)
  3. Validates ICD-10 codes via NIH Clinical Tables (fills gaps, fixes
  specificity)
  4. Checks drug safety via OpenFDA (recalls affecting patient's meds,
  interaction warnings between concurrent meds, monitoring requirements from FDA
   labels)
  5. Searches PubMed for recent clinical guidelines matching the patient's top
  diagnoses
  6. Detects formulary gaps — chronic conditions without expected medication
  classes
  7. Loads patient education from MedlinePlus for diagnoses and new medications
  8. Evaluates care gaps against USPSTF screening recommendations
  9. All of this happens asynchronously — the chart loads instantly, then
  widgets populate with API data

  The Morning Briefing aggregates this intelligence across all patients:
  weather, schedule, recall alerts, care gap counts — everything a provider
  needs at 6 AM before seeing patients.

  Not Yet Implemented

  Feature: NEW-B: Abnormal Lab Interpretation
  Why: Requires LOINC reference ranges + drug-lab cross-reference logic
  What's Needed: LOINC account credentials (free registration at
    https://loinc.org)
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  Feature: NEW-G: Differential Diagnosis Widget
  Why: Requires UMLS crosswalk for condition relationships
  What's Needed: UMLS API key (free at https://uts.nlm.nih.gov/uts/)
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  Feature: Billing UI (Today View cards)
  Why: Backend engine built, needs patient-facing billing opportunity cards
  What's Needed: Route + template work (next sprint)
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  Feature: Provider API Preferences (/settings/api)
  Why: Lower priority — functional defaults work for demo
  What's Needed: Can add after demo
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  Feature: OpenFDA API key for higher rate limits
  Why: Works without key at 40 req/min; key raises to 240/min
  What's Needed: Optional: register at https://open.fda.gov/apis/authentication/
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  Feature: PubMed API key
  Why: Works without key at 3 req/sec; key raises to 10/sec
  What's Needed: Optional: register at https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/account/
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  Feature: Virginia VIS (Vaccine Information System)
  Why: Requires state system credentials, not a public API
  What's Needed: Login credentials for Virginia VIS portal
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  Feature: PDMP (Prescription Drug Monitoring)
  Why: Requires state system credentials and likely a different integration
    approach
  What's Needed: Login credentials for Virginia PDMP

  What I Need From You (When Ready)

  1. LOINC account (free) — needed for lab reference ranges and NEW-B lab
  interpretation feature
  2. UMLS API key (free) — needed for terminology crosswalk and NEW-G
  differential diagnosis
  3. Virginia VIS credentials — needed for immunization registry integration
  4. Virginia PDMP credentials — needed for controlled substance monitoring
  5. OpenFDA API key (optional, free) — increases rate limit from 40/min to
  240/min
  6. PubMed/NCBI API key (optional, free) — increases rate limit from 3/sec to
  10/sec

  None of these block the demo. All features work with the free, unauthenticated
   API tiers. The credentials would improve rate limits and unlock additional
  features.

==================================================                              
PROJECT CONTEXT                                                                 
==================================================                              
                                                                                
CareCompanion is a Windows 11 clinical workflow platform for outpatient primary  
care. It combines:                                                              
                                                                                
- Flask web app                                                                 
- SQLite local database                                                         
- Windows background agent                                                      
- Playwright automation for NetPractice/WebPractice                             
- PyAutoGUI / pywin32 / OCR automation for Amazing Charts                       
- AutoHotkey integrations                                                       
- API-driven enrichment using free government/clinical APIs                     
- multi-user role-based architecture                                            
- patient chart view driven by parsed Clinical Summary XML                      
- local-first, cache-first, privacy-preserving architecture

      423 +        .then(function(r){return r.json();})                  
      424 +        .then(function(d){                                    
      425 +            if (d.success) location.reload();                 
      426 +            else alert(d.error || 'Failed to capture          
          +opportunity');                                                
      427 +        });                                                   
      428 +}                                                             
      429 +function dismissBillingOpp(id) {                              
      430 +    var reason = prompt('Dismiss reason (optional):');        
      431 +    if (reason === null) return;                              
      432 +    fetch('/api/billing/opportunity/' + id + '/dismiss',      
          +{method:'POST',headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'},bo 
          +dy:JSON.stringify({reason:reason})})                          
      433 +        .then(function(r){return r.json();})                  
      434 +        .then(function(d){                                    
      435 +            if (d.success) location.reload();                 
      436 +            else alert(d.error || 'Failed to dismiss');       
      437 +        });                                                   
      438 +}                                                             
      439  </script>

       42 +@login_required                                               
       43 +def capture_opportunity(opp_id):                              
       44 +    """Mark a billing opportunity as captured (provider       
          +documented and billed)."""                                    
       45 +    from models.billing import BillingOpportunity             
       46 +    opp = BillingOpportunity.query.filter_by(

       48 +    ).first()

       50 +        return jsonify({'success': False, 'error':            
          +'Opportunity not found'}), 404                                
       51 +    opp.mark_captured()                                       
       52 +    db.session.commit()                                       
       53 +    return jsonify({'success': True, 'status': opp.status})   
       54 +                                                              
       55 +

          +s', methods=['POST'])                                         
       57 +@login_required                                               
       58 +def dismiss_opportunity(opp_id):                              
       59 +    """Dismiss a billing opportunity with an optional         
          +reason."""                                                    
       60 +    from models.billing import BillingOpportunity             
       61 +    data = request.get_json(silent=True) or {}                
       62 +    opp = BillingOpportunity.query.filter_by(                 
       63 +        id=opp_id, user_id=current_user.id                    
       64 +    ).first()                                                 
       65 +    if not opp:

          +'Opportunity not found'}), 404

          +'partial']),

       97 +            'documentation': o.documentation_required or '',  
       98 +            'insurer_caveat': o.insurer_caveat or '',

      111                                                                
      112                                                                
      113  # =========================================================== 
           ===========                                                   
      114 +# NEW-B: Abnormal Lab Interpretation Assistant                
      115 +# =========================================================== 
          +===========                                                   
      116 +@intel_bp.route('/api/patient/<mrn>/lab-interpretation')      
      117 +@login_required                                               
      118 +def lab_interpretation(mrn):                                  
      119 +    """                                                       
      120 +    Return lab interpretation context: LOINC reference ranges 
          + and                                                          
      121 +    medication cross-reference for abnormal values.           
      122 +    """                                                       
      123 +    from models.labtrack import LabTrack                      
      124 +                                                              
      125 +    tracks = LabTrack.query.filter_by(                        
      126 +        user_id=current_user.id, mrn=mrn                      
      127 +    ).all()                                                   
      128 +                                                              
      129 +    if not tracks:                                            
      130 +        return jsonify({'interpretations': []})               
      131 +                                                              
      132 +    medications = PatientMedication.query.filter_by(          
      133 +        user_id=current_user.id, mrn=mrn, status='active'     
      134 +    ).all()                                                   
      135 +    med_names = [m.drug_name.split()[0].lower() for m in      
          +medications if m.drug_name]                                   
      136 +                                                              
      137 +    interpretations = []                                      
      138 +    for track in tracks:                                      
      139 +        # Get latest result                                   
      140 +        latest = None                                         
      141 +        if track.results:                                     
      142 +            sorted_results = sorted(track.results, key=lambda 
          + r: r.result_date or datetime.min, reverse=True)              
      143 +            latest = sorted_results[0] if sorted_results else 
          + None                                                         
      144 +                                                              
      145 +        if not latest or not latest.result_value:             
      146 +            continue                                          
      147 +                                                              
      148 +        # Try to parse numeric value                          
      149 +        try:                                                  
      150 +            value = float(latest.result_value.replace(',',    
          +'').strip())                                                  
      151 +        except (ValueError, TypeError):                       
      152 +            continue                                          
      153 +                                                              
      154 +        interp = {                                            
      155 +            'lab_name': track.lab_name,                       
      156 +            'value': latest.result_value,                     
      157 +            'date': latest.result_date.strftime('%m/%d/%Y')   
          +if latest.result_date else '',                                
      158 +            'status': track.status,                           
      159 +            'is_abnormal': False,                             
      160 +            'direction': '',                                  
      161 +            'context': '',                                    
      162 +            'reference_range': '',                            
      163 +            'drug_context': [],                               
      164 +        }                                                     
      165 +                                                              
      166 +        # Check against provider-set thresholds               
      167 +        if track.alert_low and value < track.alert_low:       
      168 +            interp['is_abnormal'] = True                      
      169 +            interp['direction'] = 'low'                       
      170 +        elif track.alert_high and value > track.alert_high:   
      171 +            interp['is_abnormal'] = True                      
      172 +            interp['direction'] = 'high'                      
      173 +        elif track.critical_low and value <                   
          +track.critical_low:                                           
      174 +            interp['is_abnormal'] = True                      
      175 +            interp['direction'] = 'critically low'            
      176 +        elif track.critical_high and value >                  
          +track.critical_high:                                          
      177 +            interp['is_abnormal'] = True                      
      178 +            interp['direction'] = 'critically high'           
      179 +                                                              
      180 +        if track.alert_low or track.alert_high:               
      181 +            lo = str(track.alert_low) if track.alert_low else 
          + ''                                                           
      182 +            hi = str(track.alert_high) if track.alert_high    
          +else ''                                                       
      183 +            interp['reference_range'] = f"{lo} – {hi}"        
      184 +                                                              
      185 +        # Cross-reference with medications for abnormal labs  
      186 +        if interp['is_abnormal']:                             
      187 +            # Common lab-medication associations              
      188 +            LAB_DRUG_ASSOCIATIONS = {                         
      189 +                'potassium': ['lisinopril', 'losartan',       
          +'enalapril', 'spironolactone', 'trimethoprim'],               
      190 +                'creatinine': ['lisinopril', 'losartan',      
          +'ibuprofen', 'naproxen', 'metformin'],                        
      191 +                'glucose': ['metformin', 'glipizide',         
          +'insulin', 'prednisone', 'dexamethasone'],                    
      192 +                'hemoglobin a1c': ['metformin', 'glipizide',  
          +'insulin', 'semaglutide', 'empagliflozin'],                   
      193 +                'a1c': ['metformin', 'glipizide', 'insulin',  
          +'semaglutide', 'empagliflozin'],                              
      194 +                'tsh': ['levothyroxine', 'liothyronine',      
          +'amiodarone', 'lithium'],                                     
      195 +                'alt': ['atorvastatin', 'rosuvastatin',       
          +'simvastatin', 'methotrexate', 'acetaminophen'],              
      196 +                'ast': ['atorvastatin', 'rosuvastatin',       
          +'simvastatin', 'methotrexate'],                               
      197 +                'inr': ['warfarin'],                          
      198 +                'platelets': ['warfarin', 'heparin',          
          +'valproic acid'],                                             
      199 +                'wbc': ['methotrexate', 'azathioprine',       
          +'clozapine'],                                                 
      200 +                'sodium': ['hydrochlorothiazide',             
          +'furosemide', 'carbamazepine', 'desmopressin'],               
      201 +                'magnesium': ['omeprazole', 'pantoprazole',   
          +'furosemide'],                                                
      202 +                'lithium': ['lithium'],                       
      203 +                'digoxin': ['digoxin'],                       
      204 +            }                                                 
      205 +                                                              
      206 +            lab_lower = track.lab_name.lower()                
      207 +            for lab_key, drugs in                             
          +LAB_DRUG_ASSOCIATIONS.items():                                
      208 +                if lab_key in lab_lower:                      
      209 +                    for drug in drugs:                        
      210 +                        if drug in med_names:                 
      211 +                            interp['drug_context'].append({   
      212 +                                'drug': drug.title(),         
      213 +                                'note': f"Patient is on       
          +{drug.title()} which can affect {track.lab_name} levels",     
      214 +                            })                                
      215 +                                                              
      216 +            if interp['drug_context']:                        
      217 +                interp['context'] = f"{track.lab_name} is     
          +{interp['direction']} — consider medication effect"           
      218 +            else:                                             
      219 +                interp['context'] = f"{track.lab_name} is     
          +{interp['direction']} — review clinical significance"         
      220 +                                                              
      221 +        if interp['is_abnormal'] or track.status in           
          +('critical', 'overdue'):                                      
      222 +            interpretations.append(interp)                    
      223 +                                                              
      224 +    return jsonify({'interpretations': interpretations})      
      225 +                                                              
      226 +                                                              
      227 +# ===========================================================

            monitoring)

       53 +function searchDrug() {                                       
       54 +    var q =                                                   
          +document.getElementById('drug-search').value.trim();          
       55 +    if (!q || q.length < 2) return;                           
       56 +    var btn = document.getElementById('search-btn');          
       57 +    btn.disabled = true; btn.textContent = 'Searching...';    
       58 +    var container =                                           
          +document.getElementById('drug-card-container');               
       59 +    container.innerHTML = '<div class="card"                  
          +style="min-height:500px;"><div class="card-body"              
          +style="text-align:center;padding:60px;"><span class="spinner" 
          +                                                              
          +style="display:inline-block;width:24px;height:24px;border:3px 
          + solid var(--border);border-top-color:var(--color-teal);borde 
          +r-radius:50%;animation:spin 0.8s linear infinite;"></span><p  
          +style="margin-top:12px;color:var(--text-secondary);">Looking  
          +up ' + escapeHtml(q) + '...</p></div></div>';                 
       60 +                                                              
       61 +    fetch('/api/medref/lookup?q=' + encodeURIComponent(q))    
       62 +        .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })               
       63 +        .then(function(data) {                                
       64 +            btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = 'Search'; 
       65 +            if (data.error) {                                 
       66 +                container.innerHTML = '<div class="card"><div 
          + class="card-body" style="text-align:center;padding:40px;colo 
          +r:var(--color-red);">' + escapeHtml(data.error) +             
          +'</div></div>';                                               
       67 +                return;                                       
       68 +            }                                                 
       69 +            addToHistory(q);                                  
       70 +            renderDrugCard(data, container);                  
       71 +        })                                                    
       72 +        .catch(function() {                                   
       73 +            btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = 'Search'; 
       74 +            container.innerHTML = '<div class="card"><div     
          +class="card-body" style="text-align:center;padding:40px;color 
          +:var(--color-red);">Search failed — check your                
          +connection.</div></div>';                                     
       75 +        });                                                   
       76 +}

      155 +function addToHistory(q) {                                    
      156 +    _searchHistory = _searchHistory.filter(function(h) {      
          +return h.toLowerCase() !== q.toLowerCase(); });               
      157 +    _searchHistory.unshift(q);                                
      158 +    if (_searchHistory.length > 10) _searchHistory =          
          +_searchHistory.slice(0, 10);                                  
      159 +    localStorage.setItem('medref_history',                    
          +JSON.stringify(_searchHistory));                              
      160 +    renderHistory();                                          
      161 +}                                                             
      162 +                                                              
      163 +function renderHistory() {                                    
      164 +    var el = document.getElementById('history-list');         
      165 +    if (!el) return;                                          
      166 +    if (_searchHistory.length === 0) { el.innerHTML = '<span  
          +style="color:var(--text-muted);">No recent searches</span>';  
          +return; }                                                     
      167 +    var html = '';                                            
      168 +    _searchHistory.forEach(function(h) {                      
      169 +        html += '<a href="#" onclick="event.preventDefault(); 
          +document.getElementById(\'drug-search\').value=\'' +          
          +escapeHtml(h).replace(/'/g, "\\'") + '\';searchDrug();"       
          +style="display:inline-block;margin:2px 4px 2px 0;padding:2px  
          +8px;border-radius:10px;background:var(--bg-muted,#f8fafc);fon 
          +t-size:11px;color:var(--text-primary);text-decoration:none;bo 
          +rder:1px solid var(--border,#e2e8f0);">' + escapeHtml(h) +    
          +'</a>';                                                       
      170 +    });                                                       
      171 +    el.innerHTML = html;                                      
      172 +}                                                             
      173 +                                                              
      174 +function clearResults() {                                     
      175 +    document.getElementById('drug-search').value = '';        
      176 +    document.getElementById('drug-card-container').innerHTML  
          += '<div class="card" style="min-height:500px;"><div           
          +class="card-body" style="display:flex;align-items:center;just 
          +ify-content:center;color:var(--text-secondary);"><div         
          +style="text-align:center;"><div                               
          +style="font-size:48px;margin-bottom:16px;">&#128138;</div><p  
          +style="font-size:16px;margin:0;">Search for a medication to   
          +view its profile</p></div></div></div>';                      
      177 +}                                                             
      178 +                                                              
      179 +function escapeHtml(s) {                                      
      180 +    if (!s) return '';                                        
      181 +    var d = document.createElement('div');                    
      182 +    d.textContent = s;                                        
      183 +    return d.innerHTML;                                       
      184 +}                                                             
      185 +</script>                                                     
      186 +                                                              
      187 +<style>                                                       
      188 +@keyframes spin{to{transform:rotate(360deg);}}                
      189 +</style>

       37 +    Look up a drug by name. Returns combined data from RxNorm 
          + + OpenFDA.                                                   
       38 +    Query param: q (drug name string)                         
       39 +    """                                                       
       40 +    query = request.args.get('q', '').strip()                 
       41 +    if not query or len(query) < 2:                           
       42 +        return jsonify({'error': 'Enter at least 2            
          +characters'})                                                 
       43 +                                                              
       44 +    result = {                                                
       45 +        'query': query,

          +'')                                                           
       72 +

          +RxNormService as _Rx

          ++ '/related.json?tty=BN')

          +pl[0].get('name', '')

       86 +            except Exception:                                 
       87 +                pass

       92 +                if ing and ing.get('name'):                   
       93 +                    result['generic_name'] = ing['name']      
       94 +                                                              
       95 +        else:                                                 
       96 +            # Try approximate match                           
       97 +            approx =                                          
          +_fetch_rxnorm('/approximateTerm.json?term=' +                 
          +_url_quote(query))                                            
       98 +            if approx:                                        
       99 +                candidates = (approx.get('approximateGroup')  
          +or {}).get('candidate', [])                                   
      100 +                if candidates:                                
      101 +                    rxcui = candidates[0].get('rxcui', '')    
      102 +                    result['rxcui'] = rxcui

      104 +    except Exception as e:                                    
      105 +        logger.debug('RxNorm lookup failed: %s', e)           
      106 +                                                              
      107 +    # Parse dose from concept name

      111 +        if m:

      206 +                                                              
      207 +def _fetch_rxnorm(path):                                      
      208 +    """Quick RxNorm REST fetch for endpoints not covered by   
          +RxNormService."""                                             
      209 +    import urllib.request                                     
      210 +    import json as _json                                      
      211 +    url = 'https://rxnav.nlm.nih.gov/REST' + path             
      212 +    try:                                                      
      213 +        req = urllib.request.Request(url, headers={'Accept':  
          +'application/json'})                                          
      214 +        with urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=8) as resp:  
      215 +            return _json.loads(resp.read().decode())          
      216 +    except Exception:                                         
      217 +        return None                                           
      218 +                                                              
      219 +                                                              
      220 +def _url_quote(s):                                            
      221 +    """URL-encode a string."""                                
      222 +    import urllib.parse                                       
      223 +    return urllib.parse.quote(s)

           ===========                                                   
      114 +# F17b: ICD-10 Specificity Reminder                           
      115 +# =========================================================== 
          +===========                                                   
      116 +@intel_bp.route('/api/icd10/specificity')                     
      117 +@login_required                                               
      118 +def icd10_specificity():                                      
      119 +    """                                                       
      120 +    Check if an ICD-10 code has more specific child codes     
          +available.                                                    
      121 +    Returns child codes if the current code is non-terminal.  
      122 +    """                                                       
      123 +    code = request.args.get('code', '').strip().upper()       
      124 +    if not code or len(code) < 3:                             
      125 +        return jsonify({'has_children': False, 'children':    
          +[]})                                                          
      126 +                                                              
      127 +    try:                                                      
      128 +        from app.services.api.icd10 import ICD10Service       
      129 +        svc = ICD10Service(db)                                
      130 +        children = svc.get_children(code)                     
      131 +        if children:                                          
      132 +            return jsonify({                                  
      133 +                'has_children': True,                         
      134 +                'code': code,                                 
      135 +                'children': children[:10],                    
      136 +                'message': f'More specific code available for 
          + {code}',                                                     
      137 +            })                                                
      138 +        return jsonify({'has_children': False, 'code': code,  
          +'children': []})                                              
      139 +    except Exception as e:                                    
      140 +        logger.debug('ICD-10 specificity check failed: %s',   
          +e)                                                            
      141 +        return jsonify({'has_children': False, 'children':    
          +[]})                                                          
      142 +                                                              
      143 +                                                              
      144 +# =========================================================== 
          +===========                                                   
      145  # LOINC Lab Reference Range Lookup                            
      146  # =========================================================== 
           ===========

       61 +@tools_bp.route('/cs-tracker/add', methods=['POST'])          
       62 +@login_required                                               
       63 +def cs_add():                                                 
       64 +    """Add a new controlled substance entry."""               
       65 +    data = request.get_json(silent=True) or request.form      
       66 +                                                              
       67 +    drug_name = (data.get('drug_name') or '').strip()         
       68 +    if not drug_name:                                         
       69 +        if request.is_json:                                   
       70 +            return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'Drug  
          +name required'}), 400                                         
       71 +        flash('Drug name is required.', 'error')              
       72 +        return redirect(url_for('tools.cs_tracker'))          
       73 +                                                              
       74 +    entry = ControlledSubstanceEntry(                         
       75 +        user_id=current_user.id,                              
       76 +        mrn=(data.get('mrn') or '').strip(),                  
       77 +        patient_name=(data.get('patient_name') or             
          +'').strip(),                                                  
       78 +        drug_name=drug_name,                                  
       79 +        dea_schedule=(data.get('dea_schedule') or             
          +'').strip(),                                                  
       80 +        dose=(data.get('dose') or '').strip(),                
       81 +        quantity=int(data.get('quantity') or 0),              
       82 +        days_supply=int(data.get('days_supply') or 30),       
       83 +                                                              
          +pdmp_check_interval_days=int(data.get('pdmp_interval') or     
          +90),                                                          
       84 +        uds_interval_days=int(data.get('uds_interval') or     
          +180),                                                         
       85 +        notes=(data.get('notes') or '').strip(),              
       86 +    )                                                         
       87 +                                                              
       88 +    # Auto-lookup DEA schedule via RxNorm if not provided     
       89 +    if not entry.dea_schedule:                                
       90 +        entry.dea_schedule = _lookup_dea_schedule(drug_name)  
       91 +                                                              
       92 +    # Set initial fill date if provided                       
       93 +    fill_str = (data.get('last_fill_date') or '').strip()     
       94 +    if fill_str:                                              
       95 +        try:                                                  
       96 +            entry.last_fill_date =                            
          +date.fromisoformat(fill_str)                                  
       97 +            entry.next_fill_date = entry.last_fill_date +     
          +timedelta(days=entry.days_supply)                             
       98 +        except ValueError:                                    
       99 +            pass                                              
      100 +                                                              
      101 +    db.session.add(entry)                                     
      102 +    db.session.commit()                                       
      103 +                                                              
      104 +    if request.is_json:                                       
      105 +        return jsonify({'success': True, 'id': entry.id})     
      106 +    flash(f'{drug_name} added to CS tracker.', 'success')     
      107 +    return redirect(url_for('tools.cs_tracker'))

      110 +@tools_bp.route('/cs-tracker/<int:entry_id>/fill',            
          +methods=['POST'])                                             
      111 +@login_required                                               
      112 +def cs_fill(entry_id):                                        
      113 +    """Record a new fill for a controlled substance entry.""" 
      114 +    entry = ControlledSubstanceEntry.query.filter_by(         
      115 +        id=entry_id, user_id=current_user.id                  
      116 +    ).first()                                                 
      117 +    if not entry:                                             
      118 +        return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'Entry not 
          + found'}), 404                                                
      119 +                                                              
      120 +    data = request.get_json(silent=True) or request.form      
      121 +    fill_str = (data.get('fill_date') or '').strip()          
      122 +    fill_date = date.fromisoformat(fill_str) if fill_str else 
          + date.today()                                                 
      123 +    days = int(data.get('days_supply') or entry.days_supply)  
      124 +    entry.days_supply = days                                  
      125 +    entry.record_fill(fill_date)                              
      126 +    db.session.commit()                                       
      127 +                                                              
      128 +    return jsonify({                                          
      129 +        'success': True,                                      
      130 +        'next_fill': entry.next_fill_date.isoformat() if      
          +entry.next_fill_date else '',                                 
      131 +        'days_until': entry.days_until_refill,                
      132 +    })                                                        
      133 +

      185 +                                                              
      186 +                                                              
      187 +def _lookup_dea_schedule(drug_name):                          
      188 +    """Try to determine DEA schedule from RxNorm              
          +properties."""                                                
      189 +    try:                                                      
      190 +        from app.services.api.rxnorm import RxNormService     
      191 +        svc = RxNormService(db)                               
      192 +        result = svc.get_rxcui(drug_name)                     
      193 +        if result and result.get('rxcui'):                    
      194 +            props = svc.get_properties(result['rxcui'])       
      195 +            if props:                                         
      196 +                # RxNorm concept name may include schedule    
          +info                                                          
      197 +                name = (props.get('name') or '').upper()      
      198 +                for schedule in ['SCHEDULE II', 'SCHEDULE     
          +III', 'SCHEDULE IV', 'SCHEDULE V',                            
      199 +                                 'C-II', 'C-III', 'C-IV',     
          +'C-V', 'CII', 'CIII', 'CIV', 'CV']:                           
      200 +                    if schedule in name:                      
      201 +                        return schedule.replace('SCHEDULE ',  
          +'').replace('C-', '')                                         
      202 +    except Exception:                                         
      203 +        pass                                                  
      204 +                                                              
      205 +    # Common controlled substances by name                    
      206 +    KNOWN_SCHEDULES = {                                       
      207 +        'oxycodone': 'II', 'hydrocodone': 'II', 'morphine':   
          +'II', 'fentanyl': 'II',                                       
      208 +        'methadone': 'II', 'amphetamine': 'II',               
          +'methylphenidate': 'II', 'adderall': 'II',                    
      209 +        'concerta': 'II', 'ritalin': 'II', 'oxycontin': 'II', 
          + 'percocet': 'II',                                            
      210 +        'vicodin': 'II', 'norco': 'II', 'dilaudid': 'II',     
          +'suboxone': 'III',                                            
      211 +        'buprenorphine': 'III', 'testosterone': 'III',        
          +'ketamine': 'III',                                            
      212 +        'tylenol #3': 'III', 'codeine': 'III',                
      213 +        'benzodiazepine': 'IV', 'alprazolam': 'IV',           
          +'diazepam': 'IV',                                             
      214 +        'lorazepam': 'IV', 'clonazepam': 'IV', 'zolpidem':    
          +'IV',                                                         
      215 +        'xanax': 'IV', 'valium': 'IV', 'ativan': 'IV',        
          +'klonopin': 'IV',                                             
      216 +        'ambien': 'IV', 'tramadol': 'IV', 'carisoprodol':     
          +'IV', 'soma': 'IV',                                           
      217 +        'gabapentin': 'V', 'pregabalin': 'V', 'lyrica': 'V',  
      218 +    }                                                         
      219 +    name_lower = drug_name.lower().split()[0]                 
      220 +    return KNOWN_SCHEDULES.get(name_lower, '')                
      221 +                                                              
      222 +                                                              
      223 +# =========================================================== 
          +===========                                                   
      224 +# F17: ICD-10 Coding Helper                                   
      225 +# ===========================================================
