      226 +                                                              
      227 +@tools_bp.route('/coding')                                    
      228 +@login_required                                               
      229 +def coding():                                                 
      230 +    """ICD-10 coding suggester with favorites and             
          +pairings."""                                                  
      231 +    favorites = (                                             
      232 +        CodeFavorite.query                                    
      233 +        .filter_by(user_id=current_user.id)                   
      234 +        .order_by(CodeFavorite.use_count.desc())              
      235 +        .limit(50)                                            
      236 +        .all()                                                
      237 +    )                                                         
      238 +    return render_template('coding.html',                     
          +favorites=favorites)                                          
      239 +                                                              
      240 +                                                              
      241 +@tools_bp.route('/coding/search')                             
      242 +@login_required                                               
      243 +def coding_search():                                          
      244 +    """Search ICD-10 codes with specificity hints and pairing 
          + suggestions."""                                              
      245 +    query = request.args.get('q', '').strip()                 
      246 +    if not query or len(query) < 2:                           
      247 +        return jsonify({'results': [], 'pairings': []})       
      248 +                                                              
      249 +    # Search via ICD10 service                                
      250 +    results = []                                              
      251 +    try:                                                      
      252 +        from app.services.api.icd10 import ICD10Service       
      253 +        svc = ICD10Service(db)                                
      254 +        raw = svc.search(query, max_results=15)               
      255 +        for r in raw:                                         
      256 +            code = r.get('code', '')                          
      257 +            desc = r.get('description', '')                   
      258 +            # Check specificity                               
      259 +            has_children = False                              
      260 +            if code and not code[-1].isdigit():               
      261 +                has_children = False  # Already specific      
      262 +            elif code and '.' not in code:                    
      263 +                has_children = True  # Unspecified — likely   
          +has children                                                  
      264 +                                                              
      265 +            # Check if favorited                              
      266 +            is_fav = CodeFavorite.query.filter_by(            
      267 +                user_id=current_user.id, icd10_code=code      
      268 +            ).first() is not None                             
      269 +                                                              
      270 +            results.append({                                  
      271 +                'code': code,                                 
      272 +                'description': desc,                          
      273 +                'is_billable': '.' in code,                   
      274 +                'needs_specificity': has_children or          
          +code.endswith('.9'),                                          
      275 +                'is_favorite': is_fav,                        
      276 +            })                                                
      277 +    except Exception as e:                                    
      278 +        logger.debug('Coding search failed: %s', e)           
      279 +                                                              
      280 +    # Get pairing suggestions for the first result            
      281 +    pairings = []                                             
      282 +    if results:                                               
      283 +        first_code = results[0]['code']                       
      284 +        pairings = _get_pairing_suggestions(first_code)       
      285 +                                                              
      286 +    return jsonify({'results': results, 'pairings':           
          +pairings})                                                    
      287 +                                                              
      288 +                                                              
      289 +@tools_bp.route('/coding/favorite', methods=['POST'])         
      290 +@login_required                                               
      291 +def coding_add_favorite():                                    
      292 +    """Add or remove an ICD-10 code from favorites."""        
      293 +    data = request.get_json(silent=True) or {}                
      294 +    code = (data.get('code') or '').strip()                   
      295 +    desc = (data.get('description') or '').strip()            
      296 +                                                              
      297 +    if not code:                                              
      298 +        return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'Code      
          +required'}), 400                                              
      299 +                                                              
      300 +    existing = CodeFavorite.query.filter_by(                  
      301 +        user_id=current_user.id, icd10_code=code              
      302 +    ).first()                                                 
      303 +                                                              
      304 +    if existing:                                              
      305 +        db.session.delete(existing)                           
      306 +        db.session.commit()                                   
      307 +        return jsonify({'success': True, 'action':            
          +'removed'})                                                   
      308 +                                                              
      309 +    fav = CodeFavorite(                                       
      310 +        user_id=current_user.id,                              
      311 +        icd10_code=code,                                      
      312 +        description=desc,                                     
      313 +    )                                                         
      314 +    db.session.add(fav)                                       
      315 +    db.session.commit()                                       
      316 +    return jsonify({'success': True, 'action': 'added'})      
      317 +                                                              
      318 +                                                              
      319 +@tools_bp.route('/coding/pair', methods=['POST'])             
      320 +@login_required                                               
      321 +def coding_record_pair():                                     
      322 +    """Record that two codes were used together."""           
      323 +    data = request.get_json(silent=True) or {}                
      324 +    code_a = (data.get('code_a') or '').strip()               
      325 +    code_b = (data.get('code_b') or '').strip()               
      326 +                                                              
      327 +    if not code_a or not code_b or code_a == code_b:          
      328 +        return jsonify({'success': False}), 400               
      329 +                                                              
      330 +    # Normalize order so (A,B) == (B,A)                       
      331 +    if code_a > code_b:                                       
      332 +        code_a, code_b = code_b, code_a                       
      333 +                                                              
      334 +    existing = CodePairing.query.filter_by(                   
      335 +        user_id=current_user.id, code_a=code_a, code_b=code_b 
      336 +    ).first()                                                 
      337 +                                                              
      338 +    if existing:                                              
      339 +        existing.pair_count += 1                              
      340 +        existing.last_used = datetime.now(timezone.utc)       
      341 +    else:                                                     
      342 +        pair = CodePairing(                                   
      343 +            user_id=current_user.id,                          
      344 +            code_a=code_a,                                    
      345 +            code_b=code_b,                                    
      346 +        )                                                     
      347 +        db.session.add(pair)                                  
      348 +                                                              
      349 +    db.session.commit()                                       
      350 +    return jsonify({'success': True})                         
      351 +                                                              
      352 +                                                              
      353 +@tools_bp.route('/coding/specificity')                        
      354 +@login_required                                               
      355 +def coding_specificity():                                     
      356 +    """Get more specific child codes for a given ICD-10       
          +code."""                                                      
      357 +    code = request.args.get('code', '').strip()               
      358 +    if not code:                                              
      359 +        return jsonify({'children': []})                      
      360 +                                                              
      361 +    try:                                                      
      362 +        from app.services.api.icd10 import ICD10Service       
      363 +        svc = ICD10Service(db)                                
      364 +        children = svc.get_children(code)                     
      365 +        return jsonify({'children': children or []})          
      366 +    except Exception:                                         
      367 +        return jsonify({'children': []})                      
      368 +                                                              
      369 +                                                              
      370 +def _get_pairing_suggestions(code):                           
      371 +    """Get commonly paired codes from user history and        
          +hardcoded clinical pairings."""                               
      372 +    suggestions = []                                          
      373 +                                                              
      374 +    # User's own pairing history                              
      375 +    pairs = CodePairing.query.filter(                         
      376 +        CodePairing.user_id == current_user.id,               
      377 +        db.or_(CodePairing.code_a == code, CodePairing.code_b 
          + == code)                                                     
      378 +    ).order_by(CodePairing.pair_count.desc()).limit(5).all()  
      379 +                                                              
      380 +    for p in pairs:                                           
      381 +        paired_code = p.code_b if p.code_a == code else       
          +p.code_a                                                      
      382 +        suggestions.append({                                  
      383 +            'code': paired_code,                              
      384 +            'source': 'history',                              
      385 +            'count': p.pair_count,                            
      386 +        })                                                    
      387 +                                                              
      388 +    # Common clinical pairings (evidence-based)               
      389 +    CLINICAL_PAIRINGS = {                                     
      390 +        'I10': ['I12.9', 'N18.3', 'E78.5', 'E11.9'],     #    
          +HTN → CKD, hyperlipidemia, DM2                                
      391 +        'E11': ['E11.65', 'E11.40', 'E11.22', 'G63'],     #   
          +DM2 → neuropathy, retinopathy, CKD                            
      392 +        'E78.5': ['I10', 'E11.9', 'I25.10'],               #  
          +Hyperlipidemia → HTN, DM2, CAD                                
      393 +        'I50': ['I10', 'I48.91', 'N18.3'],                 #  
          +HF → HTN, AFib, CKD                                           
      394 +        'J44': ['J96.10', 'R06.00', 'F17.210'],            #  
          +COPD → resp failure, dyspnea, nicotine                        
      395 +        'F32': ['F41.1', 'G47.00'],                        #  
          +Depression → anxiety, insomnia                                
      396 +        'F41': ['F32.1', 'G47.00'],                        #  
          +Anxiety → depression, insomnia                                
      397 +        'M54.5': ['M54.2', 'G89.29', 'M47.816'],           #  
          +Low back pain → cervicalgia, chronic pain                     
      398 +        'E03.9': ['E78.5', 'R63.5'],                       #  
          +Hypothyroidism → hyperlipidemia, weight gain                  
      399 +    }                                                         
      400 +                                                              
      401 +    code_prefix = code.split('.')[0] if '.' in code else code 
      402 +    for prefix, paired_codes in CLINICAL_PAIRINGS.items():    
      403 +        if code.startswith(prefix) or code_prefix == prefix:  
      404 +            for pc in paired_codes:                           
      405 +                if pc not in [s['code'] for s in              
          +suggestions]:                                                 
      406 +                    suggestions.append({                      
      407 +                        'code': pc,                           
      408 +                        'source': 'clinical',                 
      409 +                        'count': 0,                           
      410 +                    })                                        
      411 +                                                              
      412 +    return suggestions[:8]                                    
      413 +                                                              
      414 +                                                              
      415 +# =========================================================== 
          +===========                                                   
      416 +# F26: Prior Authorization Generator                          
      417 +# =========================================================== 
          +===========                                                   
      418 +                                                              
      419 +@tools_bp.route('/pa')                                        
      420 +@login_required                                               
      421 +def pa_index():                                               
      422 +    """Prior authorization generator and history."""          
      423 +    history = (                                               
      424 +        PriorAuthorization.query                              
      425 +        .filter_by(user_id=current_user.id)                   
      426 +        .order_by(PriorAuthorization.created_at.desc())       
      427 +        .limit(50)                                            
      428 +        .all()                                                
      429 +    )                                                         
      430 +    return render_template('pa.html', history=history)        
      431 +                                                              
      432 +                                                              
      433 +@tools_bp.route('/pa/generate', methods=['POST'])             
      434 +@login_required                                               
      435 +def pa_generate():                                            
      436 +    """Generate a PA narrative from drug + diagnosis + failed 
          + alternatives."""                                             
      437 +    data = request.get_json(silent=True) or {}                
      438 +                                                              
      439 +    drug_name = (data.get('drug_name') or '').strip()         
      440 +    diagnosis = (data.get('diagnosis') or '').strip()         
      441 +    icd10 = (data.get('icd10_code') or '').strip()            
      442 +    payer = (data.get('payer_name') or '').strip()            
      443 +    failed_alts = data.get('failed_alternatives', [])         
      444 +    justification = (data.get('justification') or '').strip() 
      445 +    mrn = (data.get('mrn') or '').strip()                     
      446 +    patient_name = (data.get('patient_name') or '').strip()   
      447 +                                                              
      448 +    if not drug_name:                                         
      449 +        return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'Drug name 
          + required'}), 400                                             
      450 +                                                              
      451 +    # Build narrative                                         
      452 +    narrative_parts = []                                      
      453 +    narrative_parts.append(                                   
      454 +        f"I am requesting prior authorization for {drug_name} 
          + for the treatment "                                          
      455 +        f"of {diagnosis or 'the patient\\'s condition'}"      
      456 +        f"{' (ICD-10: ' + icd10 + ')' if icd10 else ''}."     
      457 +    )                                                         
      458 +                                                              
      459 +    if failed_alts:                                           
      460 +        alt_names = [a.get('name', a) if isinstance(a, dict)  
          +else str(a) for a in failed_alts]                             
      461 +        narrative_parts.append(                               
      462 +            f"The patient has previously trialed and failed   
          +the following alternative therapies: "                        
      463 +            f"{', '.join(alt_names)}."                        
      464 +        )                                                     
      465 +        for alt in failed_alts:                               
      466 +            if isinstance(alt, dict) and alt.get('reason'):   
      467 +                narrative_parts.append(                       
      468 +                    f"  - {alt['name']}: discontinued due to  
          +{alt['reason']}."                                             
      469 +                )                                             
      470 +                                                              
      471 +    narrative_parts.append(                                   
      472 +        f"{drug_name} is medically necessary for this patient 
          + because "                                                    
      473 +        f"{justification or 'standard first-line therapies    
          +have been inadequate or contraindicated'}."                   
      474 +    )                                                         
      475 +                                                              
      476 +    # Enrich with RxNorm data                                 
      477 +    ndc = ''                                                  
      478 +    generic_available = False                                 
      479 +    drug_class = ''                                           
      480 +    try:                                                      
      481 +        from app.services.api.rxnorm import RxNormService     
      482 +        svc = RxNormService(db)                               
      483 +        cui_result = svc.get_rxcui(drug_name)                 
      484 +        if cui_result and cui_result.get('rxcui'):            
      485 +            rxcui = cui_result['rxcui']                       
      486 +            ndcs = svc.get_ndcs(rxcui)                        
      487 +            if ndcs and ndcs.get('ndcs'):                     
      488 +                ndc = ndcs['ndcs'][0]                         
      489 +                narrative_parts.append(f"NDC: {ndc}.")        
      490 +                                                              
      491 +            # Check for generic                               
      492 +            ing = svc.get_ingredient(rxcui)                   
      493 +            if ing and ing.get('rxcui') and ing['rxcui'] !=   
          +rxcui:                                                        
      494 +                generic_available = True                      
      495 +                                                              
      496 +        # Drug class                                          
      497 +        from app.services.api.rxclass import RxClassService   
      498 +        class_svc = RxClassService(db)                        
      499 +        classes =                                             
          +class_svc.get_classes_for_drug_name(drug_name)                
      500 +        if classes:                                           
      501 +            drug_class = classes[0].get('class_name', '')     
      502 +    except Exception:                                         
      503 +        pass                                                  
      504 +                                                              
      505 +    if generic_available:                                     
      506 +        narrative_parts.append(                               
      507 +            "A generic formulation may be available; however, 
          + the brand-name product is "                                  
      508 +            "requested due to specific clinical requirements  
          +or prior generic failure."                                    
      509 +        )                                                     
      510 +                                                              
      511 +    narrative = '\n\n'.join(narrative_parts)                  
      512 +                                                              
      513 +    # Save to database                                        
      514 +    pa = PriorAuthorization(                                  
      515 +        user_id=current_user.id,                              
      516 +        mrn=mrn,                                              
      517 +        patient_name=patient_name,                            
      518 +        drug_name=drug_name,                                  
      519 +        rxnorm_cui=cui_result['rxcui'] if 'cui_result' in     
          +dir() and cui_result else '',                                 
      520 +        ndc_code=ndc,                                         
      521 +        diagnosis=diagnosis,                                  
      522 +        icd10_code=icd10,                                     
      523 +        payer_name=payer,                                     
      524 +        failed_alternatives=json.dumps(failed_alts) if        
          +failed_alts else '',                                          
      525 +        clinical_justification=justification,                 
      526 +        generated_narrative=narrative,                        
      527 +        status='draft',                                       
      528 +    )                                                         
      529 +    db.session.add(pa)                                        
      530 +    db.session.commit()                                       
      531 +                                                              
      532 +    return jsonify({                                          
      533 +        'success': True,                                      
      534 +        'id': pa.id,                                          
      535 +        'narrative': narrative,                               
      536 +        'ndc': ndc,                                           
      537 +        'generic_available': generic_available,               
      538 +        'drug_class': drug_class,                             
      539 +    })                                                        
      540 +                                                              
      541 +                                                              
      542 +@tools_bp.route('/pa/<int:pa_id>/status', methods=['POST'])   
      543 +@login_required                                               
      544 +def pa_update_status(pa_id):                                  
      545 +    """Update PA status (submitted, approved, denied,         
          +appealed)."""                                                 
      546 +    pa = PriorAuthorization.query.filter_by(                  
      547 +        id=pa_id, user_id=current_user.id                     
      548 +    ).first()                                                 
      549 +    if not pa:                                                
      550 +        return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'PA not    
          +found'}), 404                                                 
      551 +                                                              
      552 +    data = request.get_json(silent=True) or {}                
      553 +    new_status = (data.get('status') or '').strip()           
      554 +    if new_status not in ('submitted', 'approved', 'denied',  
          +'appealed'):                                                  
      555 +        return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'Invalid   
          +status'}), 400                                                
      556 +                                                              
      557 +    pa.status = new_status                                    
      558 +    if new_status == 'submitted':                             
      559 +        pa.submitted_date = date.today()                      
      560 +    elif new_status in ('approved', 'denied'):                
      561 +        pa.decision_date = date.today()                       
      562 +    if new_status == 'denied':                                
      563 +        pa.denial_reason = (data.get('reason') or '').strip() 
      564 +    db.session.commit()                                       
      565 +                                                              
      566 +    return jsonify({'success': True, 'status': pa.status})    
      567 +                                                              
      568 +                                                              
      569 +@tools_bp.route('/pa/<int:pa_id>/appeal', methods=['POST'])   
      570 +@login_required                                               
      571 +def pa_generate_appeal(pa_id):                                
      572 +    """Generate an appeal narrative for a denied PA."""       
      573 +    pa = PriorAuthorization.query.filter_by(                  
      574 +        id=pa_id, user_id=current_user.id                     
      575 +    ).first()                                                 
      576 +    if not pa:                                                
      577 +        return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'PA not    
          +found'}), 404                                                 
      578 +                                                              
      579 +    appeal = (                                                
      580 +        f"APPEAL — Prior Authorization for                    
          +{pa.drug_name}\n\n"                                           
      581 +        f"This is an appeal of the denial decision dated      
          +{pa.decision_date or 'N/A'} "                                 
      582 +        f"for {pa.drug_name} for the treatment of             
          +{pa.diagnosis or 'the patient\\'s condition'}.\n\n"           
      583 +    )                                                         
      584 +    if pa.denial_reason:                                      
      585 +        appeal += f"The stated denial reason was:             
          +{pa.denial_reason}\n\n"                                       
      586 +                                                              
      587 +    appeal += (                                               
      588 +        f"I respectfully disagree with this determination.    
          +{pa.drug_name} remains "                                      
      589 +        f"medically necessary for this patient.\n\n"          
      590 +        f"{pa.clinical_justification or ''}\n\n"              
      591 +        f"The original prior authorization narrative is       
          +included below for reference:\n\n"                            
      592 +        f"---\n{pa.generated_narrative or ''}\n---\n\n"       
      593 +        f"I request that this denial be overturned and        
          +authorization be granted "                                    
      594 +        f"for {pa.drug_name}."                                
      595 +    )                                                         
      596 +                                                              
      597 +    pa.appeal_narrative = appeal                              
      598 +    pa.status = 'appealed'                                    
      599 +    db.session.commit()                                       
      600 +                                                              
      601 +    return jsonify({'success': True, 'appeal': appeal})

  ---
  Highest ROI Next Items

  1. Note Reformatter (F31) — daily use for every clinical note, uses existing
  RxNorm/ICD-10/LOINC services. High visibility during demo. ~4h.
  2. Follow-Up Tickler (F24) — simple CRUD task board, no API dependency. Used
  daily by provider and MA. ~3h.
  3. Post-visit billing review — extends existing billing engine to review after
   visit completion. ~2h.
  4. Referral Letter Generator (F27) — template-based letter builder. No API
  dependency. ~3h.
  5. UI polish pass — extract inline styles, standardize badges, add ARIA
  labels. ~6h.

  ---
  Biggest Bite at 99% Success Rate

  Note Reformatter (F31) + Follow-Up Tickler (F24) + Referral Letter Generator 
  (F27) — all three are:
  - Pure application logic + model + route + template (no external API
  dependencies)
  - Well-defined in the Development Guide with clear requirements
  - Built on existing patterns (models/tools.py pattern, tools hub linking
  pattern)
  - Combined ~10h of work, all completable in one autonomous prompt with no user
   input needed
  - Zero external blockers — no credentials, no API keys, no architecture
  decisions

  This would complete all Phase 7 features except AutoHotkey macros (which needs
   Windows-specific AHK testing) and bring total implemented features from ~70% 
  to ~85% of the Development Guide scope.

      176 +class ReferralLetter(db.Model):                               
      177 +    """F27: Referral letter tracking with generated letter    
          +text."""                                                      
      178 +    __tablename__ = 'referral_letter'                         
      179 +                                                              
      180 +    id = db.Column(db.Integer, primary_key=True)              
      181 +    user_id = db.Column(db.Integer,                           
          +db.ForeignKey('users.id'), nullable=False, index=True)        
      182 +    mrn = db.Column(db.String(20), default='')                
      183 +    patient_display = db.Column(db.String(200), default='')   
      184 +                                                              
      185 +    specialty = db.Column(db.String(100), nullable=False)     
      186 +    reason = db.Column(db.Text, default='')                   
      187 +    relevant_history = db.Column(db.Text, default='')         
      188 +    key_findings = db.Column(db.Text, default='')             
      189 +    current_medications = db.Column(db.Text, default='')      
      190 +    urgency = db.Column(db.String(20), default='routine')  #  
          +routine, urgent, emergent                                     
      191 +                                                              
      192 +    generated_letter = db.Column(db.Text, default='')         
      193 +                                                              
      194 +    # Tracking                                                
      195 +    referral_date = db.Column(db.Date, nullable=True)         
      196 +    consultation_received = db.Column(db.Boolean,             
          +default=False)                                                
      197 +    follow_up_date = db.Column(db.Date, nullable=True)        
      198 +    notes = db.Column(db.Text, default='')                    
      199 +                                                              
      200 +    created_at = db.Column(db.DateTime, default=lambda:       
          +datetime.now(timezone.utc))                                   
      201 +                                                              
      202 +    def __repr__(self):                                       
      203 +        return f'<Referral {self.specialty}                   
          +{self.patient_display}>'                                      
      204 +                                                              
      205 +    @property                                                 
      206 +    def is_overdue(self):                                     
      207 +        """True if referral sent > 6 weeks without            
          +consultation return."""                                       
      208 +        if self.consultation_received:                        
      209 +            return False                                      
      210 +        if not self.referral_date:                            
      211 +            return False                                      
      212 +        return (date.today() - self.referral_date).days > 42

● Update(routes\tools.py)
  ⎿  Added 242 lines
      603      db.session.commit()                                       
      604                                                                
      605      return jsonify({'success': True, 'appeal': appeal})       
      606 +                                                              
      607 +                                                              
      608 +# =========================================================== 
          +===========                                                   
      609 +# F24: Follow-Up Tickler System                               
      610 +# =========================================================== 
          +===========                                                   
      611 +                                                              
      612 +@tools_bp.route('/tickler')                                   
      613 +@login_required                                               
      614 +def tickler():                                                
      615 +    """Three-column tickler board: overdue, due today,        
          +upcoming."""                                                  
      616 +    from datetime import date as _date                        
      617 +    today_start = datetime.combine(_date.today(),             
          +datetime.min.time()).replace(tzinfo=timezone.utc)             
      618 +    today_end = datetime.combine(_date.today(),               
          +datetime.max.time()).replace(tzinfo=timezone.utc)             
      619 +                                                              
      620 +    all_open = (                                              
      621 +        Tickler.query                                         
      622 +        .filter_by(user_id=current_user.id,                   
          +is_completed=False)                                           
      623 +        .order_by(Tickler.due_date, Tickler.priority.desc())  
      624 +        .all()                                                
      625 +    )                                                         
      626 +    # Also show items assigned to this user by others         
      627 +    assigned = (                                              
      628 +        Tickler.query                                         
      629 +        .filter(                                              
      630 +            Tickler.assigned_to_user_id == current_user.id,   
      631 +            Tickler.is_completed == False,                    
      632 +            Tickler.user_id != current_user.id,               
      633 +        )                                                     
      634 +        .order_by(Tickler.due_date)                           
      635 +        .all()                                                
      636 +    )                                                         
      637 +    all_items = list({t.id: t for t in all_open +             
          +assigned}.values())                                           
      638 +                                                              
      639 +    overdue = [t for t in all_items if t.due_date and         
          +t.due_date < today_start]                                     
      640 +    today_items = [t for t in all_items if t.due_date and     
          +today_start <= t.due_date <= today_end]                       
      641 +    upcoming = [t for t in all_items if t.due_date and        
          +t.due_date > today_end]                                       
      642 +                                                              
      643 +    all_users = User.query.filter_by(is_active_account=True). 
          +order_by(User.display_name).all()                             
      644 +                                                              
      645 +    return render_template(                                   
      646 +        'tickler.html',                                       
      647 +        overdue=overdue,                                      
      648 +        today_items=today_items,                              
      649 +        upcoming=upcoming,                                    
      650 +        all_users=all_users,                                  
      651 +    )                                                         
      652 +                                                              
      653 +                                                              
      654 +@tools_bp.route('/tickler/add', methods=['POST'])             
      655 +@login_required                                               
      656 +def tickler_add():                                            
      657 +    """Add a new tickler item."""                             
      658 +    data = request.get_json(silent=True) or {}                
      659 +                                                              
      660 +    due_str = (data.get('due_date') or '').strip()            
      661 +    if not due_str:                                           
      662 +        return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'Due date  
          +required'}), 400                                              
      663 +                                                              
      664 +    try:                                                      
      665 +        due_dt = datetime.strptime(due_str,                   
          +'%Y-%m-%d').replace(tzinfo=timezone.utc)                      
      666 +    except ValueError:                                        
      667 +        return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'Invalid   
          +date format'}), 400                                           
      668 +                                                              
      669 +    assigned_to = data.get('assigned_to', '')                 
      670 +    assigned_id = int(assigned_to) if assigned_to and         
          +assigned_to.isdigit() else None                               
      671 +                                                              
      672 +    t = Tickler(                                              
      673 +        user_id=current_user.id,                              
      674 +        assigned_to_user_id=assigned_id,                      
      675 +        mrn=(data.get('mrn') or '').strip(),                  
      676 +        patient_display=(data.get('patient_display') or       
          +'').strip(),                                                  
      677 +        due_date=due_dt,                                      
      678 +        priority=(data.get('priority') or 'routine').strip(), 
      679 +        notes=(data.get('notes') or '').strip(),              
      680 +        is_recurring=bool(data.get('is_recurring')),          
      681 +                                                              
          +recurrence_interval_days=int(data.get('recurrence_days') or   
          +0) or None,                                                   
      682 +    )                                                         
      683 +    db.session.add(t)                                         
      684 +    db.session.commit()                                       
      685 +    return jsonify({'success': True, 'id': t.id})             
      686 +                                                              
      687 +                                                              
      688 +@tools_bp.route('/tickler/<int:tid>/complete',                
          +methods=['POST'])                                             
      689 +@login_required                                               
      690 +def tickler_complete(tid):                                    
      691 +    """Mark a tickler as completed. If recurring, create the  
          +next one."""                                                  
      692 +    t = Tickler.query.filter(                                 
      693 +        Tickler.id == tid,                                    
      694 +        db.or_(Tickler.user_id == current_user.id,            
          +Tickler.assigned_to_user_id == current_user.id)               
      695 +    ).first()                                                 
      696 +    if not t:                                                 
      697 +        return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'Not       
          +found'}), 404                                                 
      698 +                                                              
      699 +    t.is_completed = True                                     
      700 +    t.completed_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)               
      701 +                                                              
      702 +    # Auto-create next occurrence if recurring                
      703 +    if t.is_recurring and t.recurrence_interval_days:         
      704 +        next_due = t.due_date +                               
          +timedelta(days=t.recurrence_interval_days)                    
      705 +        next_t = Tickler(                                     
      706 +            user_id=t.user_id,                                
      707 +            assigned_to_user_id=t.assigned_to_user_id,        
      708 +            mrn=t.mrn,                                        
      709 +            patient_display=t.patient_display,                
      710 +            due_date=next_due,                                
      711 +            priority=t.priority,                              
      712 +            notes=t.notes,                                    
      713 +            is_recurring=True,                                
      714 +                                                              
          +recurrence_interval_days=t.recurrence_interval_days,          
      715 +        )                                                     
      716 +        db.session.add(next_t)                                
      717 +                                                              
      718 +    db.session.commit()                                       
      719 +    return jsonify({'success': True})                         
      720 +                                                              
      721 +                                                              
      722 +@tools_bp.route('/tickler/<int:tid>/snooze',                  
          +methods=['POST'])                                             
      723 +@login_required                                               
      724 +def tickler_snooze(tid):                                      
      725 +    """Snooze a tickler to a new date."""                     
      726 +    t = Tickler.query.filter(                                 
      727 +        Tickler.id == tid,                                    
      728 +        db.or_(Tickler.user_id == current_user.id,            
          +Tickler.assigned_to_user_id == current_user.id)               
      729 +    ).first()                                                 
      730 +    if not t:                                                 
      731 +        return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'Not       
          +found'}), 404                                                 
      732 +                                                              
      733 +    data = request.get_json(silent=True) or {}                
      734 +    days = int(data.get('days') or 7)                         
      735 +    t.due_date = datetime.now(timezone.utc) +                 
          +timedelta(days=days)                                          
      736 +    db.session.commit()                                       
      737 +    return jsonify({'success': True})                         
      738 +                                                              
      739 +                                                              
      740 +# =========================================================== 
          +===========                                                   
      741 +# F27: Referral Letter Generator                              
      742 +# =========================================================== 
          +===========                                                   
      743 +                                                              
      744 +SPECIALTIES = [                                               
      745 +    'Cardiology', 'Orthopedics', 'Gastroenterology',          
          +'Dermatology',                                                
      746 +    'Endocrinology', 'Neurology', 'Urology', 'Pulmonology',   
      747 +    'Nephrology', 'Rheumatology', 'Psychiatry', 'General      
          +Surgery',                                                     
      748 +    'Ophthalmology', 'ENT/Otolaryngology',                    
          +'Allergy/Immunology',                                         
      749 +    'Hematology/Oncology', 'Infectious Disease', 'Pain        
          +Management',                                                  
      750 +    'Physical Medicine', 'Podiatry', 'Other',                 
      751 +]                                                             
      752 +                                                              
      753 +                                                              
      754 +@tools_bp.route('/referral')                                  
      755 +@login_required                                               
      756 +def referral():                                               
      757 +    """Referral letter generator and tracking log."""         
      758 +    log = (                                                   
      759 +        ReferralLetter.query                                  
      760 +        .filter_by(user_id=current_user.id)                   
      761 +        .order_by(ReferralLetter.created_at.desc())           
      762 +        .limit(50)                                            
      763 +        .all()                                                
      764 +    )                                                         
      765 +    return render_template('referral.html', log=log,          
          +specialties=SPECIALTIES)                                      
      766 +                                                              
      767 +                                                              
      768 +@tools_bp.route('/referral/generate', methods=['POST'])       
      769 +@login_required                                               
      770 +def referral_generate():                                      
      771 +    """Generate a referral letter and save to log."""         
      772 +    data = request.get_json(silent=True) or {}                
      773 +                                                              
      774 +    specialty = (data.get('specialty') or '').strip()         
      775 +    reason = (data.get('reason') or '').strip()               
      776 +    history = (data.get('relevant_history') or '').strip()    
      777 +    findings = (data.get('key_findings') or '').strip()       
      778 +    meds = (data.get('current_medications') or '').strip()    
      779 +    urgency = (data.get('urgency') or 'routine').strip()      
      780 +    patient = (data.get('patient_display') or 'this           
          +patient').strip()                                             
      781 +                                                              
      782 +    if not specialty or not reason:                           
      783 +        return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'Specialty 
          + and reason required'}), 400                                  
      784 +                                                              
      785 +    # Get provider name from user profile                     
      786 +    provider_name = current_user.display_name or              
          +current_user.username                                         
      787 +                                                              
      788 +    # Generate letter                                         
      789 +    today_str = date.today().strftime('%B %d, %Y')            
      790 +    urgency_line = ''                                         
      791 +    if urgency == 'urgent':                                   
      792 +        urgency_line = '\n**URGENT REFERRAL — Please expedite 
          + scheduling.**\n'                                             
      793 +    elif urgency == 'emergent':                               
      794 +        urgency_line = '\n**EMERGENT REFERRAL — Same-day      
          +evaluation requested.**\n'                                    
      795 +                                                              
      796 +    letter = f"""{today_str}                                  
      797 +                                                              
      798 +Dear {specialty} Colleague,                                   
      799 +{urgency_line}                                                
      800 +I am referring {patient} for evaluation of {reason}.          
      801 +                                                              
      802 +"""                                                           
      803 +    if history:                                               
      804 +        letter += f"RELEVANT HISTORY:\n{history}\n\n"         
      805 +    if findings:                                              
      806 +        letter += f"KEY CLINICAL FINDINGS:\n{findings}\n\n"   
      807 +    if meds:                                                  
      808 +        letter += f"CURRENT MEDICATIONS:\n{meds}\n\n"         
      809 +                                                              
      810 +    letter += f"""I would appreciate your evaluation and      
          +recommendations regarding the management of this patient.     
          +Please send a consultation note to our office at your         
          +earliest convenience.                                         
      811 +                                                              
      812 +Thank you for your expertise and timely attention.            
      813 +                                                              
      814 +Sincerely,                                                    
      815 +{provider_name}                                               
      816 +Family Practice Associates of Chesterfield"""                 
      817 +                                                              
      818 +    ref = ReferralLetter(                                     
      819 +        user_id=current_user.id,                              
      820 +        mrn=(data.get('mrn') or '').strip(),                  
      821 +        patient_display=patient,                              
      822 +        specialty=specialty,                                  
      823 +        reason=reason,                                        
      824 +        relevant_history=history,                             
      825 +        key_findings=findings,                                
      826 +        current_medications=meds,                             
      827 +        urgency=urgency,                                      
      828 +        generated_letter=letter,                              
      829 +        referral_date=date.today(),                           
      830 +    )                                                         
      831 +    db.session.add(ref)                                       
      832 +    db.session.commit()                                       
      833 +                                                              
      834 +    return jsonify({'success': True, 'id': ref.id, 'letter':  
          +letter})                                                      
      835 +                                                              
      836 +                                                              
      837 +@tools_bp.route('/referral/<int:ref_id>/received',            
          +methods=['POST'])                                             
      838 +@login_required                                               
      839 +def referral_received(ref_id):                                
      840 +    """Mark a referral consultation as received."""           
      841 +    ref = ReferralLetter.query.filter_by(id=ref_id,           
          +user_id=current_user.id).first()                              
      842 +    if not ref:                                               
      843 +        return jsonify({'success': False}), 404               
      844 +    ref.consultation_received = True                          
      845 +    ref.follow_up_date = date.today()                         
      846 +    db.session.commit()                                       
      847 +    return jsonify({'success': True})

● Yes — that's both reasonable and high-value. A medical terminology fuzzy
  matcher that flags likely clinical terms in free text (misspelled diagnoses,
  abbreviations, slang) and lets the provider confirm/correct them is exactly
  the kind of feature that separates a data display from a clinical decision
  support tool. The approval workflow prevents silent errors while still saving
  time.

  now.

● Write(app\services\clinical_spell_check.py)
  ⎿  Wrote 534 lines to app\services\clinical_spell_check.py
     """
     CareCompanion — Clinical Terminology Spell Check & Fuzzy Matcher
     File: app/services/clinical_spell_check.py

     Provides medical-aware spell checking and fuzzy matching for free text
     in clinical notes. Handles:
     - Medical abbreviations (HTN, DM2, GERD, CHF, CKD, etc.)
     - Clinical slang (nitro, dig, lytes, chem, bili, etc.)
     - Misspelled drug names (fuzzy match against RxNorm)
     - Misspelled diagnoses (fuzzy match against ICD-10 descriptions)
     … +524 lines (ctrl+o to expand)

● Now add the spell check API endpoint to the intelligence routes:

● Read 1 file (ctrl+o to expand)

● Update(routes\intelligence.py)
  ⎿  Added 76 lines
      101                                                                
      102                                                                
      103  # =========================================================== 
           ===========                                                   
      104 +# Clinical Spell Check / Fuzzy Matcher                        
      105 +# =========================================================== 
          +===========                                                   
      106 +@intel_bp.route('/api/spell-check', methods=['POST'])         
      107 +@login_required                                               
      108 +def spell_check():                                            
      109 +    """                                                       
      110 +    Analyze free text for medical terminology issues:         
          +abbreviations,                                                
      111 +    misspellings, drug name fuzzy matches, diagnosis fuzzy    
          +matches.                                                      
      112 +    Returns findings with confidence scores for provider      
          +review.                                                       
      113 +    """                                                       
      114 +    data = request.get_json(silent=True) or {}                
      115 +    text = (data.get('text') or '').strip()                   
      116 +    use_api = data.get('use_api', True)                       
      117 +                                                              
      118 +    if not text:                                              
      119 +        return jsonify({'findings': []})                      
      120 +                                                              
      121 +    try:                                                      
      122 +        from app.services.clinical_spell_check import         
          +analyze_text                                                  
      123 +        findings = analyze_text(text, use_api=use_api)        
      124 +        return jsonify({                                      
      125 +            'findings': findings,                             
      126 +            'total': len(findings),                           
      127 +            'high_confidence': len([f for f in findings if    
          +f['confidence'] >= 0.85]),                                    
      128 +            'needs_review': len([f for f in findings if 0.6   
          +<= f['confidence'] < 0.85]),                                  
      129 +        })                                                    
      130 +    except Exception as e:                                    
      131 +        logger.debug('Spell check failed: %s', e)             
      132 +        return jsonify({'findings': [], 'error': str(e)})     
      133 +                                                              
      134 +                                                              
      135 +@intel_bp.route('/api/spell-check/expand', methods=['POST'])  
      136 +@login_required                                               
      137 +def spell_check_expand():                                     
      138 +    """Expand a single medical abbreviation."""               
      139 +    data = request.get_json(silent=True) or {}                
      140 +    abbrev = (data.get('abbreviation') or '').strip()         
      141 +    if not abbrev:                                            
      142 +        return jsonify({'expansion': None})                   
      143 +                                                              
      144 +    from app.services.clinical_spell_check import             
          +expand_abbreviation                                           
      145 +    expansion = expand_abbreviation(abbrev)                   
      146 +    return jsonify({'abbreviation': abbrev, 'expansion':      
          +expansion})                                                   
      147 +                                                              
      148 +                                                              
      149 +# =========================================================== 
          +===========                                                   
      150 +# Post-Visit Billing Review                                   
      151 +# =========================================================== 
          +===========                                                   
      152 +@intel_bp.route('/billing/review/<mrn>')                      
      153 +@login_required                                               
      154 +def billing_review(mrn):                                      
      155 +    """Post-visit billing review for a specific patient."""   
      156 +    from models.billing import BillingOpportunity             
      157 +                                                              
      158 +    opportunities = (                                         
      159 +        BillingOpportunity.query                              
      160 +        .filter_by(user_id=current_user.id)                   
      161 +        .filter(BillingOpportunity.patient_mrn_hash.like(f'%{ 
          +mrn[-6:]}%') if len(mrn) > 6 else                             
          +BillingOpportunity.patient_mrn_hash != '')                    
      162 +        .order_by(BillingOpportunity.visit_date.desc())       
      163 +        .limit(20)                                            
      164 +        .all()                                                
      165 +    )                                                         
      166 +                                                              
      167 +    record = PatientRecord.query.filter_by(                   
      168 +        user_id=current_user.id, mrn=mrn                      
      169 +    ).first()                                                 
      170 +                                                              
      171 +    return render_template(                                   
      172 +        'billing_review.html',                                
      173 +        mrn=mrn,                                              
      174 +        record=record,                                        
      175 +        opportunities=opportunities,                          
      176 +    )                                                         
      177 +                                                              
      178 +                                                              
      179 +# =========================================================== 
          +===========                                                   
      180  # API Setup Guide (accessible to all authenticated users)     
      181  # =========================================================== 
           ===========

      1232 +/* ---- Clinical Terminology Spell Check ---- */             
      1233 +function runSpellCheck() {                                   
      1234 +    var btn = document.getElementById('spell-check-btn');    
      1235 +    var resultsEl =                                          
           +document.getElementById('spell-check-results');              
      1236 +    btn.disabled = true; btn.textContent = 'Checking...';    
      1237 +                                                             
      1238 +    // Collect all note section text                         
      1239 +    var allText = '';                                        
      1240 +    document.querySelectorAll('#note-sections                
           +textarea').forEach(function(ta) {                            
      1241 +        allText += ta.value + '\n';                          
      1242 +    });                                                      
      1243 +                                                             
      1244 +    if (!allText.trim()) {                                   
      1245 +        btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = '\u{1F50D}   
           +Check Terminology';                                          
      1246 +        resultsEl.style.display = 'block';                   
      1247 +        resultsEl.innerHTML = '<div                          
           +style="color:var(--text-secondary);text-align:center;">No    
           +note text to check.</div>';                                  
      1248 +        return;                                              
      1249 +    }                                                        
      1250 +                                                             
      1251 +    fetch('/api/spell-check', {                              
      1252 +        method: 'POST',                                      
      1253 +        headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'},       
      1254 +        body: JSON.stringify({text: allText, use_api: true}) 
      1255 +    })                                                       
      1256 +    .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })                  
      1257 +    .then(function(data) {                                   
      1258 +        btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = '\u{1F50D}   
           +Check Terminology';                                          
      1259 +        var findings = data.findings || [];                  
      1260 +        resultsEl.style.display = 'block';                   
      1261 +                                                             
      1262 +        if (findings.length === 0) {                         
      1263 +            resultsEl.innerHTML = '<div style="color:var(--c 
           +olor-green);text-align:center;padding:8px;">\u2713 No        
           +terminology issues found. All terms recognized.</div>';      
      1264 +            return;                                          
      1265 +        }                                                    
      1266 +                                                             
      1267 +        var html = '<div                                     
           +style="font-weight:600;margin-bottom:8px;">Found ' +         
           +findings.length + ' terminology item(s):</div>';             
      1268 +        html += '<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text 
           +-secondary);margin-bottom:8px;">High confidence (\u226585%)  
           +items can be auto-accepted. Medium confidence (60-85%) items 
           + need your review.</div>';                                   
      1269 +                                                             
      1270 +        findings.forEach(function(f, i) {                    
      1271 +            var confColor = f.confidence >= 0.85 ?           
           +'var(--color-green)' : f.confidence >= 0.7 ?                 
           +'var(--color-warning)' : 'var(--text-secondary)';            
      1272 +            var confPct = Math.round(f.confidence * 100);    
      1273 +            var catLabel = {'abbreviation':'Abbreviation','m 
           +isspelling':'Misspelling','drug_fuzzy':'Drug                 
           +Match','diagnosis_fuzzy':'Diagnosis Match'}[f.category] ||   
           +f.category;                                                  
      1274 +                                                             
      1275 +            html += '<div style="padding:8px;margin:4px      
           +0;background:var(--bg-surface,#fff);border:1px solid         
           +var(--border);border-radius:4px;display:flex;align-items:cen 
           +ter;gap:10px;">';                                            
      1276 +            html += '<div style="flex:1;">';                 
      1277 +            html += '<span style="font-weight:600;color:var( 
           +--color-red);text-decoration:line-through;">' +              
           +escHtml(f.original) + '</span>';                             
      1278 +            html += ' \u2192 <span                           
           +style="font-weight:600;color:var(--color-green);">' +        
           +escHtml(f.suggested) + '</span>';                            
      1279 +            html += '<div style="font-size:10px;color:var(-- 
           +text-secondary);margin-top:2px;">';                          
      1280 +            html += '<span class="badge"                     
           +style="font-size:9px;padding:1px                             
           +5px;border-radius:6px;background:var(--bg-muted);color:' +   
           +confColor + ';">' + catLabel + ' ' + confPct + '%</span>';   
      1281 +            if (f.context) html += ' <span                   
           +style="font-style:italic;">"' +                              
           +escHtml(f.context).substring(0, 60) + '"</span>';            
      1282 +            html += '</div></div>';                          
      1283 +            html += '<button class="btn btn-sm btn-primary"  
           +style="font-size:10px;" onclick="acceptSpellFix(' + i +      
           +',\'' + escHtml(f.original).replace(/'/g, "\\'") + '\',\'' + 
           + escHtml(f.suggested).replace(/'/g, "\\'") +                 
           +'\')">Accept</button>';

           +style="font-size:10px;" onclick="this.parentElement.style.di

      1285 +            html += '</div>';                                
      1286 +        });

      1289 +    })                                                       
      1290 +    .catch(function() {                                      
      1291 +        btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = '\u{1F50D}   
           +Check Terminology';                                          
      1292 +        resultsEl.style.display = 'block';                   
      1293 +        resultsEl.innerHTML = '<div                          
           +style="color:var(--color-red);text-align:center;">Spell      
           +check service unavailable.</div>';                           
      1294 +    });                                                      
      1295 +}                                                            
      1296 +                                                             
      1297 +function acceptSpellFix(idx, original, suggested) {          
      1298 +    // Replace the original text with the suggestion in all  
           +note textareas                                               
      1299 +    document.querySelectorAll('#note-sections                
           +textarea').forEach(function(ta) {                            
      1300 +        if (ta.value.indexOf(original) !== -1) {             
      1301 +            ta.value =                                       
           +ta.value.split(original).join(suggested);                    
      1302 +        }                                                    
      1303 +    });                                                      
      1304 +    // Remove the finding card                               
      1305 +    var cards =                                              
           +document.querySelectorAll('#spell-check-results > div >      
           +div');                                                       
      1306 +    // Just re-run the check to refresh                      
      1307 +    showNoteStatus('Applied: ' + original + ' \u2192 ' +     
           +suggested, 'success');                                       
      1308 +}
