      1935  | You now have everything you need to build this. Start with 
             Phase 1, Feature 1\. One step at a time. |                  
      1936  | :---: |                                                    
      1937                                                               
      1938 +---                                                          
      1939 +                                                             
      1940 +## ADDENDUM: Feature F32 — Clinical Terminology Spell Check  
           +& Fuzzy Matcher                                              
      1941 +                                                             
      1942 +**Added:** 2026-03-18 (CL23 API Intelligence Build)          
      1943 +**Phase:** 10A (Intelligence Layer)                          
      1944 +**Status:** Implemented                                      
      1945 +                                                             
      1946 +### Overview                                                 
      1947 +                                                             
      1948 +Medical-aware spell checking and fuzzy matching for free     
           +text in clinical notes. Handles misspelled drug names,       
           +diagnoses, medical abbreviations, and clinical slang.        
           +Provider-approved corrections prevent silent errors while    
           +saving documentation time.                                   
      1949 +                                                             
      1950 +### How It Works                                             
      1951 +                                                             
      1952 +1. **Text Analysis** — When provider clicks "Check           
           +Terminology" in the Note Generator widget, all note section  
           +text is sent to the spell check service (no PHI leaves the   
           +system — only the text content).                             
      1953 +                                                             
      1954 +2. **Multi-Layer Matching:**                                 
      1955 +   - **Layer 1 — Abbreviation Dictionary** (~200 entries):   
           +Exact-match medical abbreviations (HTN→hypertension,         
           +DM2→type 2 diabetes mellitus, CTAB→clear to auscultation     
           +bilaterally, etc.)                                           
      1956 +   - **Layer 2 — Known Misspelling Dictionary** (~100        
           +entries): Common clinical misspellings                       
           +(lisinipril→lisinopril, hypothyriodism→hypothyroidism, etc.) 
      1957 +   - **Layer 3 — Local Fuzzy Match**: Python                 
           +`difflib.SequenceMatcher` against combined dictionaries      
           +(cutoff 0.75)                                                
      1958 +   - **Layer 4 — RxNorm API Fuzzy Match**: For unresolved 6+ 
           + character words that look clinical, queries RxNorm          
           +`getSpellingSuggestions` endpoint                            
      1959 +                                                             
      1960 +3. **Confidence Scoring:**                                   
      1961 +   - **High (≥85%)** — abbreviation exact matches, known     
           +misspelling matches → auto-accept recommended                
      1962 +   - **Medium (60-85%)** — fuzzy matches → flagged for       
           +provider review                                              
      1963 +   - **Below 60%** — filtered out to prevent false positives 
      1964 +                                                             
      1965 +4. **Provider Approval Workflow:**                           
      1966 +   - Each finding shows: original word, suggested            
           +correction, confidence score, context, category              
      1967 +   - Provider clicks "Accept" to apply correction to note    
           +text, or "Ignore" to skip                                    
      1968 +   - Corrections are applied in-place to the note textarea   
           +content                                                      
      1969 +                                                             
      1970 +### Routes                                                   
      1971 +                                                             
      1972 +| Route | Method | Purpose |                                 
      1973 +|-------|--------|---------|                                 
      1974 +| `/api/spell-check` | POST | Analyze text, return findings  
           +with confidence scores |                                     
      1975 +| `/api/spell-check/expand` | POST | Expand a single         
           +abbreviation |                                               
      1976 +                                                             
      1977 +### Files                                                    
      1978 +                                                             
      1979 +| File | Purpose |                                           
      1980 +|------|---------|                                           
      1981 +| `app/services/clinical_spell_check.py` | Core matching     
           +engine with dictionaries |                                   
      1982 +| `routes/intelligence.py` | API endpoints |                 
      1983 +| `templates/patient_chart.html` | "Check Terminology"       
           +button + results UI in Note Generator widget |               
      1984 +                                                             
      1985 +### Dictionary Categories                                    
      1986 +                                                             
      1987 +| Category | Count | Examples |                              
      1988 +|----------|-------|---------|                               
      1989 +| Diagnosis abbreviations | ~70 | HTN, DM2, CHF, CKD, COPD,  
           +GERD, BPH, OSA |                                             
      1990 +| Clinical shorthand | ~50 | yo, hx, sx, tx, rx, dx, prn,    
           +bid, tid, qid |                                              
      1991 +| Physical exam terms | ~20 | WNL, NAD, CTAB, RRR, NTND,     
           +PERRLA, EOMI |                                               
      1992 +| Drug abbreviations | ~30 | ASA, APAP, NSAID, ACEI, ARB,    
           +CCB, SSRI, PPI |                                             
      1993 +| Lab abbreviations | ~30 | CBC, BMP, CMP, LFTs, TFTs, A1c,  
           +TSH, INR |                                                   
      1994 +| Drug misspellings | ~50 | lisinipril, metforman,           
           +atorvistatin, gabapenton |                                   
      1995 +| Diagnosis misspellings | ~40 | hypertention, diabeties,    
           +hypothyriodism, nueropathy |                                 
      1996 +                                                             
      1997 +### Safety Notes                                             
      1998 +                                                             
      1999 +- No patient identifiers are included in the text analysis   
      2000 +- The spell check service runs locally — no text is sent to  
           +external APIs                                                
      2001 +- RxNorm fuzzy matching (Layer 4) sends only individual      
           +words, never patient context                                 
      2002 +- All corrections require explicit provider approval — no    
           +auto-correction without consent                              
      2003 +- Abbreviation expansion is informational; original          
           +abbreviation is preserved if provider prefers                
      2004 +

      189 +function refilterCard() {                                     
      190 +    // When pregnancy/renal/hepatic filters change,           
          +re-highlight relevant sections                                
      191 +    var pregnancy =                                           
          +document.getElementById('filter-pregnancy').checked;          
      192 +    var renal =                                               
          +document.getElementById('filter-renal').checked;              
      193 +    var hepatic =                                             
          +document.getElementById('filter-hepatic').checked;            
      194 +                                                              
      195 +    // Find all label sections in the drug card and           
          +auto-expand filtered ones                                     
      196 +    var container =                                           
          +document.getElementById('drug-card-container');               
      197 +    if (!container) return;                                   
      198 +                                                              
      199 +    var sections =                                            
          +container.querySelectorAll('[data-section-key]');             
      200 +    sections.forEach(function(sec) {                          
      201 +        var key = sec.getAttribute('data-section-key');       
      202 +        var content = sec.querySelector('.section-content');  
      203 +        var header = sec.querySelector('.section-header');    
      204 +        var shouldHighlight = false;                          
      205 +                                                              
      206 +        if (pregnancy && (key === 'pregnancy'))               
          +shouldHighlight = true;                                       
      207 +        if (renal && (key === 'renal_hepatic'))               
          +shouldHighlight = true;                                       
      208 +        if (hepatic && (key === 'renal_hepatic'))             
          +shouldHighlight = true;                                       
      209 +                                                              
      210 +        if (shouldHighlight) {                                
      211 +            sec.style.background = 'rgba(220,38,38,0.08)';    
      212 +            sec.style.borderLeft = '3px solid                 
          +var(--color-red,#e74c3c)';                                    
      213 +            if (content) content.style.display = 'block';     
      214 +        } else {                                              
      215 +            sec.style.background = '';                        
      216 +            sec.style.borderLeft = '';                        
      217 +        }                                                     
      218 +    });                                                       
      219 +}

      193      except Exception as e:

      196 +    # 6. F10d: RxNorm history status — check for              
          +obsoleted/remapped drugs                                      
      197 +    result['guideline_flag'] = None                           
      198 +    if rxcui:                                                 
      199 +        try:                                                  
      200 +            history = _fetch_rxnorm('/rxcui/' + rxcui +       
          +'/historystatus.json')                                        
      201 +            if history:                                       
      202 +                status_info =                                 
          +(history.get('rxcuiStatusHistory') or {}).get('metaData') or  
          +{}                                                            
      203 +                status = (status_info.get('status') or        
          +'').lower()                                                   
      204 +                if status in ('remapped', 'obsolete',         
          +'retired'):                                                   
      205 +                    remapped_to = ''                          
      206 +                    remapped_data =                           
          +(history.get('rxcuiStatusHistory') or                         
          +{}).get('derivedConcepts') or {}                              
      207 +                    remapped_list =                           
          +remapped_data.get('remappedConcept', [])                      
      208 +                    if remapped_list and                      
          +isinstance(remapped_list, list):                              
      209 +                        remapped_to =                         
          +remapped_list[0].get('remappedRxCui', '')                     
      210 +                    result['guideline_flag'] = {              
      211 +                        'status': status,                     
      212 +                        'message': f'This drug entry has been 
          + {status} in the RxNorm database. Prescribing information may 
          + be outdated.',                                               
      213 +                        'remapped_to': remapped_to,           
      214 +                    }                                         
      215 +        except Exception:                                     
      216 +            pass                                              
      217 +                                                              
      218      # If we got no data at all, return error                  
      219      if not result['rxcui'] and not result['label'] and not    
           result['generic_name']:                                       
      220          return jsonify({'error': f'No results found for       
           "{query}". Try a different spelling or generic name.'})

● Item 3: Scheduling Intelligence — AWV/CCM eligibility analysis for the
  dashboard:

● Searched for 2 patterns, read 1 file (ctrl+o to expand)

● Update(routes\intelligence.py)
  ⎿  Added 78 lines
      177                                                                
      178                                                                
      179  # =========================================================== 
           ===========                                                   
      180 +# Scheduling Intelligence — AWV/CCM eligibility analysis      
      181 +# =========================================================== 
          +===========                                                   
      182 +@intel_bp.route('/api/scheduling-intelligence')               
      183 +@login_required                                               
      184 +def scheduling_intelligence():                                
      185 +    """                                                       
      186 +    Analyze the provider's patient panel for scheduling       
          +opportunities:                                                
      187 +    - AWV candidates: Medicare patients with >12 months since 
          + last AWV                                                     
      188 +    - CCM candidates: Patients with 2+ chronic conditions not 
          + enrolled in CCM                                              
      189 +    Returns lists of patients who should be scheduled.        
      190 +    """                                                       
      191 +    from app.api_config import CCM_CHRONIC_CONDITION_PREFIXES 
      192 +                                                              
      193 +    claimed = PatientRecord.query.filter_by(                  
      194 +        claimed_by=current_user.id                            
      195 +    ).all()                                                   
      196 +                                                              
      197 +    if not claimed:                                           
      198 +        return jsonify({'awv_candidates': [],                 
          +'ccm_candidates': [], 'total_panel': 0})                      
      199 +                                                              
      200 +    awv_candidates = []                                       
      201 +    ccm_candidates = []                                       
      202 +                                                              
      203 +    for record in claimed:                                    
      204 +        mrn = record.mrn                                      
      205 +        diagnoses = PatientDiagnosis.query.filter_by(         
      206 +            user_id=current_user.id, mrn=mrn, status='active' 
      207 +        ).all()                                               
      208 +                                                              
      209 +        icd_codes = [d.icd10_code or '' for d in diagnoses]   
      210 +                                                              
      211 +        # AWV check: any patient with insurer_type containing 
          + 'medicare'                                                   
      212 +        insurer = (getattr(record, 'insurer_type', '') or     
          +'').lower()                                                   
      213 +        if 'medicare' in insurer or not insurer:              
      214 +            last_awv = getattr(record, 'last_awv_date', None) 
      215 +            months_since = None                               
      216 +            if last_awv:                                      
      217 +                from datetime import date as _d               
      218 +                delta = _d.today() - last_awv                 
      219 +                months_since = delta.days / 30.44             
      220 +            if last_awv is None or (months_since and          
          +months_since >= 11):                                          
      221 +                awv_candidates.append({                       
      222 +                    'mrn': mrn,                               
      223 +                    'name': record.patient_name or 'Unknown', 
      224 +                    'months_since_awv': round(months_since,   
          +1) if months_since else None,                                 
      225 +                    'reason': 'No AWV on record' if not       
          +last_awv else f'{round(months_since, 0):.0f} months since     
          +last AWV',                                                    
      226 +                })                                            
      227 +                                                              
      228 +        # CCM check: 2+ chronic conditions                    
      229 +        chronic_count = 0                                     
      230 +        chronic_names = []                                    
      231 +        for code in icd_codes:                                
      232 +            for prefix in CCM_CHRONIC_CONDITION_PREFIXES:     
      233 +                if code.upper().startswith(prefix):           
      234 +                    chronic_count += 1                        
      235 +                    dx = next((d for d in diagnoses if        
          +d.icd10_code == code), None)                                  
      236 +                    if dx:                                    
      237 +                                                              
          +chronic_names.append(dx.diagnosis_name or code)               
      238 +                    break                                     
      239 +                                                              
      240 +        ccm_enrolled = getattr(record, 'ccm_enrolled', False) 
      241 +        if chronic_count >= 2 and not ccm_enrolled:           
      242 +            ccm_candidates.append({                           
      243 +                'mrn': mrn,                                   
      244 +                'name': record.patient_name or 'Unknown',     
      245 +                'chronic_count': chronic_count,               
      246 +                'conditions': chronic_names[:5],              
      247 +                'reason': f'{chronic_count} chronic           
          +conditions — CCM eligible',                                   
      248 +            })                                                
      249 +                                                              
      250 +    return jsonify({                                          
      251 +        'awv_candidates': awv_candidates[:20],                
      252 +        'ccm_candidates': ccm_candidates[:20],                
      253 +        'total_panel': len(claimed),                          
      254 +    })                                                        
      255 +                                                              
      256 +                                                              
      257 +# =========================================================== 
          +===========                                                   
      258  # API Setup Guide (accessible to all authenticated users)     
      259  # =========================================================== 
           ===========                                                   
      260  @intel_bp.route('/api-setup-guide')

      177                                                                
      178                                                                
      179  # =========================================================== 
           ===========                                                   
      180 +# F31 Step 2: Note Section Parser (standalone, no AC          
          +dependency)                                                   
      181 +# =========================================================== 
          +===========                                                   
      182 +@intel_bp.route('/api/parse-note', methods=['POST'])          
      183 +@login_required                                               
      184 +def parse_note():                                             
      185 +    """                                                       
      186 +    Parse free text into clinical note sections.              
      187 +    Used by the Note Reformatter wizard and the spell check   
          +feature.                                                      
      188 +    """                                                       
      189 +    data = request.get_json(silent=True) or {}                
      190 +    text = (data.get('text') or '').strip()                   
      191 +                                                              
      192 +    if not text:                                              
      193 +        return jsonify({'sections': {}, 'summary': 'No text   
          +provided'})                                                   
      194 +                                                              
      195 +    try:                                                      
      196 +        from agent.note_parser import parse_note_sections,    
          +get_section_summary                                           
      197 +        parsed = parse_note_sections(text)                    
      198 +        summary = get_section_summary(parsed)                 
      199 +                                                              
      200 +        # Extract metadata before returning                   
      201 +        meta = parsed.pop('_metadata', {})                    
      202 +        needs_review = parsed.pop('needs_review', [])         
      203 +        unclassified = parsed.pop('unclassified_text', '')    
      204 +                                                              
      205 +        return jsonify({                                      
      206 +            'sections': parsed,                               
      207 +            'unclassified_text': unclassified,                
      208 +            'needs_review': needs_review,                     
      209 +            'metadata': meta,                                 
      210 +            'summary': summary,                               
      211 +        })                                                    
      212 +    except Exception as e:                                    
      213 +        logger.debug('Note parse failed: %s', e)              
      214 +        return jsonify({'sections': {}, 'error': str(e)})     
      215 +                                                              
      216 +                                                              
      217 +# =========================================================== 
          +===========                                                   
      218  # Scheduling Intelligence — AWV/CCM eligibility analysis      
      219  # =========================================================== 
           ===========

      177                                                                
      178                                                                
      179  # =========================================================== 
           ===========                                                   
      180 +# F31: Note Reformatter Wizard (full pipeline)                
      181 +# =========================================================== 
          +===========                                                   
      182 +@intel_bp.route('/reformatter')                               
      183 +@login_required                                               
      184 +def reformatter():                                            
      185 +    """Note Reformatter wizard — paste text, parse, classify, 
          + review, output."""                                           
      186 +    return render_template('reformatter.html')                
      187 +                                                              
      188 +                                                              
      189 +@intel_bp.route('/api/reformat-note', methods=['POST'])       
      190 +@login_required                                               
      191 +def api_reformat_note():                                      
      192 +    """                                                       
      193 +    Complete reformatter pipeline: parse → classify →         
          +template fill.                                                
      194 +    Returns filled note, flagged items, and coverage stats.   
      195 +    """                                                       
      196 +    data = request.get_json(silent=True) or {}                
      197 +    text = (data.get('text') or '').strip()                   
      198 +    use_api = data.get('use_api', False)                      
      199 +                                                              
      200 +    if not text:                                              
      201 +        return jsonify({'error': 'No text provided'})         
      202 +                                                              
      203 +    try:                                                      
      204 +        from agent.note_reformatter import reformat_note      
      205 +        result = reformat_note(text, use_api=use_api)         
      206 +        return jsonify(result)                                
      207 +    except Exception as e:                                    
      208 +        logger.debug('Reformat failed: %s', e)                
      209 +        return jsonify({'error': str(e)})                     
      210 +                                                              
      211 +                                                              
      212 +@intel_bp.route('/api/reformat-note/resolve-flag',            
          +methods=['POST'])                                             
      213 +@login_required                                               
      214 +def resolve_flag():                                           
      215 +    """                                                       
      216 +    Resolve a flagged item from the reformatter:              
      217 +    action = 'add_to_section' | 'keep_as_text' | 'discard'    
      218 +    """                                                       
      219 +    data = request.get_json(silent=True) or {}                
      220 +    # This endpoint exists for the audit trail — the actual   
          +text                                                          
      221 +    # manipulation happens client-side. We log the decision.  
      222 +    action = data.get('action', '')                           
      223 +    flagged_text = data.get('text', '')                       
      224 +    section = data.get('section', '')                         
      225 +                                                              
      226 +    if action == 'discard':                                   
      227 +        # Log discarded items for audit trail                 
      228 +        from models.reformatter import ReformatLog            
      229 +        logger.info(                                          
      230 +            'Reformatter: user %s discarded flagged item from 
          + section %s: %s',                                             
      231 +            current_user.id, section, flagged_text[:100]      
      232 +        )                                                     
      233 +                                                              
      234 +    return jsonify({'success': True, 'action': action})       
      235 +                                                              
      236 +                                                              
      237 +# =========================================================== 
          +===========                                                   
      238  # F31 Step 2: Note Section Parser (standalone, no AC          
           dependency)                                                   
      239  # =========================================================== 
           ===========                                                   
      240  @intel_bp.route('/api/parse-note', methods=['POST'])

  ---
  Highest ROI Next Items

  1. PDMP Playwright scraper — automated controlled substance monitoring from CS
   Tracker. High compliance value, uses stored credentials. ~6h.
  2. F29 Practice Admin View — multi-provider analytics. Shows total panel size,
   care gap compliance %, billing capture rate, productivity metrics across
  providers. ~4h.
  3. F31 Template Builder — drag-drop UI for custom note section ordering. Makes
   the reformatter personalizable. ~3h.
  4. UI polish pass — extract inline styles to CSS classes, standardize badges,
  add ARIA labels. ~6h.
  5. Test suite — pytest fixtures for routes, models, API services. ~8h.

  ---
  Biggest Bite at 99% Success Rate

  PDMP Playwright scraper + F29 Practice Admin View + F31 Template Builder —
  combined ~13 human-hours:

  - PDMP scraper: Playwright login to virginia.pmpaware.net using stored
  credentials, navigate to patient search, extract prescription history, display
   in CS Tracker (6h)
  - Practice Admin View: aggregate metrics across all providers — panel sizes,
  care gap %, billing opportunities captured, overdue labs, referral return
  rates. New route + template. (4h)
  - F31 Template Builder: drag-drop section reordering, save template as JSON to
   user preferences, load in reformatter. (3h)

  All use existing patterns and credentials. The PDMP scraper follows the same
  Playwright architecture as the NetPractice scraper. Zero new external
  dependencies.

      153 +@tools_bp.route('/cs-tracker/<int:entry_id>/pdmp-lookup',     
          +methods=['POST'])                                             
      154 +@login_required                                               
      155 +def cs_pdmp_lookup(entry_id):                                 
      156 +    """Run an automated PDMP lookup for a CS tracker          
          +patient."""                                                   
      157 +    entry = ControlledSubstanceEntry.query.filter_by(         
      158 +        id=entry_id, user_id=current_user.id                  
      159 +    ).first()                                                 
      160 +    if not entry:                                             
      161 +        return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'Entry not 
          + found'}), 404                                                
      162 +                                                              
      163 +    # Get patient record for name/DOB                         
      164 +    from models.patient import PatientRecord                  
      165 +    patient = PatientRecord.query.filter_by(                  
      166 +        user_id=current_user.id, mrn=entry.mrn                
      167 +    ).first() if entry.mrn else None                          
      168 +                                                              
      169 +    if not patient or not patient.patient_name:               
      170 +        return jsonify({                                      
      171 +            'success': False,                                 
      172 +            'error': 'Patient name and DOB required for PDMP  
          +lookup. Update patient demographics first.',                  
      173 +        })                                                    
      174 +                                                              
      175 +    # Parse name into first/last                              
      176 +    name_parts = (patient.patient_name or '').split(',')      
      177 +    if len(name_parts) >= 2:                                  
      178 +        last_name = name_parts[0].strip()                     
      179 +        first_name = name_parts[1].strip().split()[0] if      
          +name_parts[1].strip() else ''                                 
      180 +    else:                                                     
      181 +        parts = patient.patient_name.split()                  
      182 +        first_name = parts[0] if parts else ''                
      183 +        last_name = parts[-1] if len(parts) > 1 else ''       
      184 +                                                              
      185 +    # Parse DOB                                               
      186 +    dob_raw = patient.patient_dob or ''                       
      187 +    dob_clean = dob_raw.replace('-', '').replace('/', '')     
      188 +    if len(dob_clean) >= 8:                                   
      189 +        dob =                                                 
          +f'{dob_clean[:4]}-{dob_clean[4:6]}-{dob_clean[6:8]}'          
      190 +    else:                                                     
      191 +        dob = dob_raw                                         
      192 +                                                              
      193 +    if not first_name or not last_name:                       
      194 +        return jsonify({'success': False, 'error': 'Could not 
          + parse patient name'})                                        
      195 +                                                              
      196 +    try:                                                      
      197 +        import asyncio                                        
      198 +        from flask import current_app                         
      199 +        from scrapers.pdmp import PDMPScraper                 
      200 +        scraper =                                             
          +PDMPScraper(current_app._get_current_object())                
      201 +        result =                                              
          +asyncio.run(scraper.lookup_patient(first_name, last_name,     
          +dob))                                                         
      202 +                                                              
      203 +        # Record the PDMP check regardless of success         
      204 +        entry.last_pdmp_check = date.today()                  
      205 +        db.session.commit()                                   
      206 +                                                              
      207 +        return jsonify(result)                                
      208 +    except Exception as e:                                    
      209 +        return jsonify({                                      
      210 +            'success': False,                                 
      211 +            'error': f'PDMP lookup failed: {str(e)}',         
      212 +            'prescriptions': [],                              
      213 +        })

      152 +function autoPDMP(id) {                                       
      153 +    if (!confirm('Run automated PDMP lookup for this          
          +patient?\nThis will connect to virginia.pmpaware.net.'))      
          +return;                                                       
      154 +    var btn = event.target;                                   
      155 +    btn.disabled = true; btn.textContent = 'Checking...';     
      156 +    fetch('/cs-tracker/' + id + '/pdmp-lookup',               
          +{method:'POST',headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}})  
      157 +        .then(function(r){return r.json();})                  
      158 +        .then(function(d){                                    
      159 +            btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = 'Auto';   
      160 +            if (d.success && d.prescriptions &&               
          +d.prescriptions.length > 0) {                                 
      161 +                var msg = 'PDMP Results (' +                  
          +d.prescriptions.length + ' prescription(s)):\n\n';            
      162 +                d.prescriptions.forEach(function(rx) {        
      163 +                    msg += rx.date_filled + ' | ' +           
          +rx.drug_name + ' | Qty: ' + rx.quantity + ' | ' +             
          +rx.days_supply + 'd | ' + rx.prescriber + '\n';               
      164 +                });                                           
      165 +                alert(msg);                                   
      166 +                location.reload();                            
      167 +            } else if (d.success) {                           
      168 +                alert('PDMP check complete — no controlled    
          +substance prescriptions found.');                             
      169 +                location.reload();                            
      170 +            } else {                                          
      171 +                alert('PDMP lookup: ' + (d.error || 'Unknown  
          +error'));                                                     
      172 +            }                                                 
      173 +        })                                                    
      174 +        .catch(function(){                                    
      175 +            btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = 'Auto';   
      176 +            alert('PDMP connection failed');                  
      177 +        });                                                   
      178 +}                                                             
      179  </script>

● Update(routes\admin.py)
  ⎿  Added 120 lines
       55                                                                
       56                                                                
       57  # =========================================================== 
           ===========                                                   
       58 +# GET /admin/practice — Practice-wide analytics (F29)         
       59 +# =========================================================== 
          +===========                                                   
       60 +@admin_bp.route('/admin/practice')                            
       61 +@login_required                                               
       62 +@_require_admin                                               
       63 +def practice_overview():                                      
       64 +    """Multi-provider practice analytics dashboard."""        
       65 +    from models.patient import PatientRecord,                 
          +PatientDiagnosis                                              
       66 +    from models.caregap import CareGap                        
       67 +    from models.labtrack import LabTrack                      
       68 +    from models.tools import ControlledSubstanceEntry,        
          +ReferralLetter                                                
       69 +    from models.billing import BillingOpportunity             
       70 +                                                              
       71 +    # Aggregate metrics                                       
       72 +    all_providers =                                           
          +User.query.filter_by(is_active_account=True,                  
          +role='provider').all()                                        
       73 +    if not all_providers:                                     
       74 +        all_providers =                                       
          +User.query.filter_by(is_active_account=True).all()            
       75 +                                                              
       76 +    total_patients = PatientRecord.query.count()              
       77 +    active_providers = len(all_providers)                     
       78 +                                                              
       79 +    all_gaps = CareGap.query.all()                            
       80 +    total_open_gaps = sum(1 for g in all_gaps if not          
          +g.is_addressed)                                               
       81 +    total_addressed = sum(1 for g in all_gaps if              
          +g.is_addressed)                                               
       82 +    total_gaps = len(all_gaps)                                
       83 +    gap_compliance_pct = round(total_addressed / total_gaps * 
          + 100) if total_gaps > 0 else 100                              
       84 +                                                              
       85 +    overdue_labs = LabTrack.query.filter(                     
       86 +        LabTrack.status.in_(['overdue', 'critical'])          
       87 +    ).count()                                                 
       88 +                                                              
       89 +    overdue_referrals = ReferralLetter.query.filter_by(       
       90 +        consultation_received=False                           
       91 +    ).count()                                                 
       92 +    # Only count those >6 weeks old                           
       93 +    from datetime import timedelta as _td                     
       94 +    cutoff = date.today() - _td(days=42)                      
       95 +    overdue_referrals = ReferralLetter.query.filter(          
       96 +        ReferralLetter.consultation_received == False,        
       97 +        ReferralLetter.referral_date.isnot(None),             
       98 +        ReferralLetter.referral_date <= cutoff,               
       99 +    ).count()                                                 
      100 +                                                              
      101 +    # Per-provider stats                                      
      102 +    provider_stats = []                                       
      103 +    for prov in all_providers:                                
      104 +        panel =                                               
          +PatientRecord.query.filter_by(claimed_by=prov.id).count()     
      105 +        p_gaps =                                              
          +CareGap.query.filter_by(user_id=prov.id).all()                
      106 +        p_open = sum(1 for g in p_gaps if not g.is_addressed) 
      107 +        p_total = len(p_gaps)                                 
      108 +        p_compliance = round((p_total - p_open) / p_total *   
          +100) if p_total > 0 else 100                                  
      109 +                                                              
      110 +        p_overdue_labs = LabTrack.query.filter(               
      111 +            LabTrack.user_id == prov.id,                      
      112 +            LabTrack.status.in_(['overdue', 'critical'])      
      113 +        ).count()                                             
      114 +                                                              
      115 +        p_overdue_refs = ReferralLetter.query.filter(         
      116 +            ReferralLetter.user_id == prov.id,                
      117 +            ReferralLetter.consultation_received == False,    
      118 +            ReferralLetter.referral_date.isnot(None),         
      119 +            ReferralLetter.referral_date <= cutoff,           
      120 +        ).count()                                             
      121 +                                                              
      122 +        p_billing = BillingOpportunity.query.filter_by(       
      123 +            user_id=prov.id, status='pending'                 
      124 +        ).count()                                             
      125 +                                                              
      126 +        p_cs = ControlledSubstanceEntry.query.filter_by(      
      127 +            user_id=prov.id, is_active=True                   
      128 +        ).count()                                             
      129 +                                                              
      130 +        provider_stats.append({                               
      131 +            'name': prov.display_name or prov.username,       
      132 +            'panel_size': panel,                              
      133 +            'open_gaps': p_open,                              
      134 +            'gap_compliance': p_compliance,                   
      135 +            'overdue_labs': p_overdue_labs,                   
      136 +            'overdue_referrals': p_overdue_refs,              
      137 +            'billing_pending': p_billing,                     
      138 +            'cs_patients': p_cs,                              
      139 +        })                                                    
      140 +                                                              
      141 +    # Gap compliance by type                                  
      142 +    gap_types = {}                                            
      143 +    for g in all_gaps:                                        
      144 +        gt = g.gap_type or g.gap_name or 'Unknown'            
      145 +        if gt not in gap_types:                               
      146 +            gap_types[gt] = {'total': 0, 'addressed': 0,      
          +'open': 0}                                                    
      147 +        gap_types[gt]['total'] += 1                           
      148 +        if g.is_addressed:                                    
      149 +            gap_types[gt]['addressed'] += 1                   
      150 +        else:                                                 
      151 +            gap_types[gt]['open'] += 1                        
      152 +                                                              
      153 +    gap_by_type = []                                          
      154 +    for gt, counts in sorted(gap_types.items()):              
      155 +        pct = round(counts['addressed'] / counts['total'] *   
          +100) if counts['total'] > 0 else 0                            
      156 +        gap_by_type.append({                                  
      157 +            'type': gt,                                       
      158 +            'total': counts['total'],                         
      159 +            'addressed': counts['addressed'],                 
      160 +            'open': counts['open'],                           
      161 +            'pct': pct,                                       
      162 +        })                                                    
      163 +                                                              
      164 +    return render_template(                                   
      165 +        'admin_practice.html',                                
      166 +        total_patients=total_patients,                        
      167 +        active_providers=active_providers,                    
      168 +        total_open_gaps=total_open_gaps,                      
      169 +        gap_compliance_pct=gap_compliance_pct,                
      170 +        overdue_labs=overdue_labs,                            
      171 +        overdue_referrals=overdue_referrals,                  
      172 +        provider_stats=provider_stats,                        
      173 +        gap_by_type=gap_by_type,                              
      174 +    )                                                         
      175 +                                                              
      176 +                                                              
      177 +# =========================================================== 
          +===========                                                   
      178  # GET /admin/sitemap — Developer Site Map                     
      179  # =========================================================== 
           ===========                                                   
      180  @admin_bp.route('/admin/sitemap')

      189 +@intel_bp.route('/api/save-note-template', methods=['POST'])  
      190 +@login_required                                               
      191 +def save_note_template():                                     
      192 +    """Save user's custom note template to preferences."""    
      193 +    data = request.get_json(silent=True) or {}                
      194 +    template = data.get('template', {})                       
      195 +    if template:                                              
      196 +        import json as _json                                  
      197 +        current_user.set_pref('note_template',                
          +_json.dumps(template))                                        
      198 +        db.session.commit()                                   
      199 +    return jsonify({'success': True})                         
      200 +

          +===========
